844    /// I64 comparison with.
845    fn emit_cmpop_i64_dynamic_b(
846        &mut self,
847        c: Condition,
848        loc_a: Location,
849        loc_b: Location,
850        ret: Location,
851    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
852        match ret {
853            Location::GPR(_) => {
854                self.emit_relaxed_cmp(Size::S64, loc_b, loc_a)?;
855                self.assembler.emit_cset(Size::S32, ret, c)?;
856            }
857            Location::Memory(_, _) => {
858                let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
859                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
860                })?;
861                self.emit_relaxed_cmp(Size::S64, loc_b, loc_a)?;
862                self.assembler.emit_cset(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp), c)?;
863                self.move_location(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp), ret)?;
864                self.release_gpr(tmp);
865            }
866            _ => {
867                codegen_error!("singlepass emit_compop_i64_dynamic_b unreachable");
868            }
869        }
870        Ok(())
871    }
872    /// I32 comparison with.
873    fn emit_cmpop_i32_dynamic_b(
874        &mut self,
875        c: Condition,
876        loc_a: Location,
877        loc_b: Location,
878        ret: Location,
879    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
880        match ret {
881            Location::GPR(_) => {
882                self.emit_relaxed_cmp(Size::S32, loc_b, loc_a)?;
883                self.assembler.emit_cset(Size::S32, ret, c)?;
884            }
885            Location::Memory(_, _) => {
886                let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
887                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
888                })?;
889                self.emit_relaxed_cmp(Size::S32, loc_b, loc_a)?;
890                self.assembler.emit_cset(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp), c)?;
891                self.move_location(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp), ret)?;
892                self.release_gpr(tmp);
893            }
894            _ => {
895                codegen_error!("singlepass emit_cmpop_i32_dynamic_b unreachable");
896            }
897        }
898        Ok(())
899    }
900
901    #[allow(clippy::too_many_arguments)]
902    fn memory_op<F: FnOnce(&mut Self, GPR) -> Result<(), CompileError>>(
903        &mut self,
904        addr: Location,
905        memarg: &MemArg,
906        check_alignment: bool,
907        value_size: usize,
908        need_check: bool,
909        imported_memories: bool,
910        offset: i32,
911        heap_access_oob: Label,
912        unaligned_atomic: Label,
913        cb: F,
914    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
915        let tmp_addr = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
916            CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
917        })?;
918
919        // Reusing `tmp_addr` for temporary indirection here, since it's not used before the last reference to `{base,bound}_loc`.
920        let (base_loc, bound_loc) = if imported_memories {
921            // Imported memories require one level of indirection.
922            self.emit_relaxed_binop(
923                Assembler::emit_mov,
924                Size::S64,
925                Location::Memory(self.get_vmctx_reg(), offset),
926                Location::GPR(tmp_addr),
927                true,
928            )?;
929            (Location::Memory(tmp_addr, 0), Location::Memory(tmp_addr, 8))
930        } else {
931            (
932                Location::Memory(self.get_vmctx_reg(), offset),
933                Location::Memory(self.get_vmctx_reg(), offset + 8),
934            )
935        };
936
937        let tmp_base = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
938            CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
939        })?;
940        let tmp_bound = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
941            CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
942        })?;
943
944        // Load base into temporary register.
945        self.emit_relaxed_ldr64(Size::S64, Location::GPR(tmp_base), base_loc)?;
946
947        // Load bound into temporary register, if needed.
948        if need_check {
949            self.emit_relaxed_ldr64(Size::S64, Location::GPR(tmp_bound), bound_loc)?;
950
951            // Wasm -> Effective.
952            // Assuming we never underflow - should always be true on Linux/macOS and Windows >=8,
953            // since the first page from 0x0 to 0x1000 is not accepted by mmap.
954            self.assembler.emit_add(
955                Size::S64,
956                Location::GPR(tmp_bound),
957                Location::GPR(tmp_base),
958                Location::GPR(tmp_bound),
959            )?;
960            if self.compatible_imm(value_size as _, ImmType::Bits12) {
961                self.assembler.emit_sub(
962                    Size::S64,
963                    Location::GPR(tmp_bound),
964                    Location::Imm32(value_size as _),
965                    Location::GPR(tmp_bound),
966                )?;
967            } else {
968                let tmp2 = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
969                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
970                })?;
971                self.assembler
972                    .emit_mov_imm(Location::GPR(tmp2), value_size as u64)?;
973                self.assembler.emit_sub(
974                    Size::S64,
975                    Location::GPR(tmp_bound),
976                    Location::GPR(tmp2),
977                    Location::GPR(tmp_bound),
978                )?;
979                self.release_gpr(tmp2);
980            }
981        }
982
983        // Load effective address.
984        // `base_loc` and `bound_loc` becomes INVALID after this line, because `tmp_addr`
985        // might be reused.
986        self.move_location(Size::S32, addr, Location::GPR(tmp_addr))?;
987
988        // Add offset to memory address.
989        if memarg.offset != 0 {
990            if self.compatible_imm(memarg.offset as _, ImmType::Bits12) {
991                self.assembler.emit_adds(
992                    Size::S32,
993                    Location::Imm32(memarg.offset as u32),
994                    Location::GPR(tmp_addr),
995                    Location::GPR(tmp_addr),
996                )?;
997            } else {
998                let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
999                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
1000                })?;
1001                self.assembler
1002                    .emit_mov_imm(Location::GPR(tmp), memarg.offset as _)?;
1003                self.assembler.emit_adds(
1004                    Size::S32,
1005                    Location::GPR(tmp_addr),
1006                    Location::GPR(tmp),
1007                    Location::GPR(tmp_addr),
1008                )?;
1009                self.release_gpr(tmp);
1010            }
1011
1012            // Trap if offset calculation overflowed.
1013            self.assembler
1014                .emit_bcond_label_far(Condition::Cs, heap_access_oob)?;
1015        }
1016
1017        // Wasm linear memory -> real memory
1018        self.assembler.emit_add(
1019            Size::S64,
1020            Location::GPR(tmp_base),
1021            Location::GPR(tmp_addr),
1022            Location::GPR(tmp_addr),
1023        )?;
1024
1025        if need_check {
1026            // Trap if the end address of the requested area is above that of the linear memory.
1027            self.assembler.emit_cmp(
1028                Size::S64,
1029                Location::GPR(tmp_bound),
1030                Location::GPR(tmp_addr),
1031            )?;
1032
1033            // `tmp_bound` is inclusive. So trap only if `tmp_addr > tmp_bound`.
1034            self.assembler
1035                .emit_bcond_label_far(Condition::Hi, heap_access_oob)?;
1036        }
1037
1038        self.release_gpr(tmp_bound);
1039        self.release_gpr(tmp_base);
1040
1041        let align = value_size as u32;
1042        if check_alignment && align != 1 {
1043            self.assembler.emit_tst(
1044                Size::S64,
1045                Location::Imm32(align - 1),
1046                Location::GPR(tmp_addr),
1047            )?;
1048            self.assembler
1049                .emit_bcond_label_far(Condition::Ne, unaligned_atomic)?;
1050        }
1051        let begin = self.assembler.get_offset().0;
1052        cb(self, tmp_addr)?;
1053        let end = self.assembler.get_offset().0;
1054        self.mark_address_range_with_trap_code(TrapCode::HeapAccessOutOfBounds, begin, end);
1055
1056        self.release_gpr(tmp_addr);
1057        Ok(())
1058    }
1059
1060    fn offset_is_ok(&self, size: Size, offset: i32) -> bool {
1061        if offset < 0 {
1062            return false;
1063        }
1064        let shift = match size {
1065            Size::S8 => 0,
1066            Size::S16 => 1,
1067            Size::S32 => 2,
1068            Size::S64 => 3,
1069        };
1070        if offset >= 0x1000 << shift {
1071            return false;
1072        }
1073        if (offset & ((1 << shift) - 1)) != 0 {
1074            return false;
1075        }
1076        true
1077    }
1078
1079    fn emit_push(&mut self, sz: Size, src: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
1080        match (sz, src) {
1081            (Size::S64, Location::GPR(_)) | (Size::S64, Location::SIMD(_)) => {
1082                let offset = if self.pushed {
1083                    0
1084                } else {
1085                    self.assembler.emit_sub(
1086                        Size::S64,
1087                        Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp),
1088                        Location::Imm8(16),
1089                        Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp),
1090                    )?;
1091                    8
1092                };
1093                self.assembler
1094                    .emit_stur(Size::S64, src, GPR::XzrSp, offset)?;
1095                self.pushed = !self.pushed;
1096            }
1097            (Size::S64, _) => {
1098                let mut temps = vec![];
1099                let src = self.location_to_reg(sz, src, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
1100                let offset = if self.pushed {
1101                    0
1102                } else {
1103                    self.assembler.emit_sub(
1104                        Size::S64,
1105                        Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp),
1106                        Location::Imm8(16),
1107                        Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp),
1108                    )?;
1109                    8
1110                };
1111                self.assembler
1112                    .emit_stur(Size::S64, src, GPR::XzrSp, offset)?;
1113                self.pushed = !self.pushed;
1114                for r in temps {
1115                    self.release_gpr(r);
1116                }
1117            }
1118            _ => codegen_error!("singlepass can't emit PUSH {:?} {:?}", sz, src),
1119        }
1120        Ok(())
1121    }
1122    fn emit_double_push(
1123        &mut self,
1124        sz: Size,
1125        src1: Location,
1126        src2: Location,
1127    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
1128        if !self.pushed {
1129            match (sz, src1, src2) {
1130                (Size::S64, Location::GPR(_), Location::GPR(_)) => {
1131                    self.assembler
1132                        .emit_stpdb(Size::S64, src1, src2, GPR::XzrSp, 16)?;
1133                }
1134                _ => {
1135                    self.emit_push(sz, src1)?;
1136                    self.emit_push(sz, src2)?;
1137                }
1138            }
1139        } else {
1140            self.emit_push(sz, src1)?;
1141            self.emit_push(sz, src2)?;
1142        }
1143        Ok(())
1144    }
1145    fn emit_pop(&mut self, sz: Size, dst: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
1146        match (sz, dst) {
1147            (Size::S64, Location::GPR(_)) | (Size::S64, Location::SIMD(_)) => {
1148                let offset = if self.pushed { 8 } else { 0 };
1149                self.assembler
1150                    .emit_ldur(Size::S64, dst, GPR::XzrSp, offset)?;
1151                if self.pushed {
1152                    self.assembler.emit_add(
1153                        Size::S64,
1154                        Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp),
1155                        Location::Imm8(16),
1156                        Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp),
1157                    )?;
1158                }
1159                self.pushed = !self.pushed;
1160            }
1161            _ => codegen_error!("singlepass can't emit POP {:?} {:?}", sz, dst),
1162        }
1163        Ok(())
1164    }
1165    fn emit_double_pop(
1166        &mut self,
1167        sz: Size,
1168        dst1: Location,
1169        dst2: Location,
1170    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
1171        if !self.pushed {
1172            match (sz, dst1, dst2) {
1173                (Size::S64, Location::GPR(_), Location::GPR(_)) => {
1174                    self.assembler
1175                        .emit_ldpia(Size::S64, dst1, dst2, GPR::XzrSp, 16)?;
1176                }
1177                _ => {
1178                    self.emit_pop(sz, dst2)?;
1179                    self.emit_pop(sz, dst1)?;
1180                }
1181            }
1182        } else {
1183            self.emit_pop(sz, dst2)?;
1184            self.emit_pop(sz, dst1)?;
1185        }
1186        Ok(())
1187    }
1188
1189    fn set_default_nan(&mut self, temps: &mut Vec<GPR>) -> Result<GPR, CompileError> {
1190        // temporarly set FPCR to DefaultNan
1191        let old_fpcr = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
1192            CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
1193        })?;
1194        temps.push(old_fpcr);
1195        self.assembler.emit_read_fpcr(old_fpcr)?;
1196        let new_fpcr = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
1197            CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
1198        })?;
1199        temps.push(new_fpcr);
1200        let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
1201            CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
1202        })?;
1203        temps.push(tmp);
1204        self.assembler
1205            .emit_mov(Size::S32, Location::Imm32(1), Location::GPR(tmp))?;
1206        self.assembler
1207            .emit_mov(Size::S64, Location::GPR(old_fpcr), Location::GPR(new_fpcr))?;
1208        // DN is bit 25 of FPCR
1209        self.assembler.emit_bfi(
1210            Size::S64,
1211            Location::GPR(tmp),
1212            25,
1213            1,
1214            Location::GPR(new_fpcr),
1215        )?;
1216        self.assembler.emit_write_fpcr(new_fpcr)?;
1217        Ok(old_fpcr)
1218    }
1219    fn set_trap_enabled(&mut self, temps: &mut Vec<GPR>) -> Result<GPR, CompileError> {
1220        // temporarly set FPCR to DefaultNan
1221        let old_fpcr = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
1222            CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
1223        })?;
1224        temps.push(old_fpcr);
1225        self.assembler.emit_read_fpcr(old_fpcr)?;
1226        let new_fpcr = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
1227            CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
1228        })?;
1229        temps.push(new_fpcr);
1230        self.assembler
1231            .emit_mov(Size::S64, Location::GPR(old_fpcr), Location::GPR(new_fpcr))?;
1232        // IOE is bit 8 of FPCR
1233        self.assembler
1234            .emit_bfc(Size::S64, 8, 1, Location::GPR(new_fpcr))?;
1235        self.assembler.emit_write_fpcr(new_fpcr)?;
1236        Ok(old_fpcr)
1237    }
1238    fn restore_fpcr(&mut self, old_fpcr: GPR) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
1239        self.assembler.emit_write_fpcr(old_fpcr)
1240    }
1241
1242    fn reset_exception_fpsr(&mut self) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
1243        // reset exception count in FPSR
1244        let fpsr = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
1245            CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
1246        })?;
1247        self.assembler.emit_read_fpsr(fpsr)?;
1248        // IOC is 0
1249        self.assembler
1250            .emit_bfc(Size::S64, 0, 1, Location::GPR(fpsr))?;
1251        self.assembler.emit_write_fpsr(fpsr)?;
1252        self.release_gpr(fpsr);
1253        Ok(())
1254    }
1255    fn read_fpsr(&mut self) -> Result<GPR, CompileError> {
1256        let fpsr = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
1257            CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
1258        })?;
1259        self.assembler.emit_read_fpsr(fpsr)?;
1260        Ok(fpsr)
1261    }
1262
1263    fn trap_float_convertion_errors(
1264        &mut self,
1265        old_fpcr: GPR,
1266        sz: Size,
1267        f: Location,
1268        temps: &mut Vec<GPR>,
1269    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
1270        let trap_badconv = self.assembler.get_label();
1271        let end = self.assembler.get_label();
1272
1273        let fpsr = self.read_fpsr()?;
1274        temps.push(fpsr);
1275        // no trap, than all good
1276        self.assembler
1277            .emit_tbz_label(Size::S32, Location::GPR(fpsr), 0, end)?;
1278        // now need to check if it's overflow or NaN
1279        self.assembler
1280            .emit_bfc(Size::S64, 0, 4, Location::GPR(fpsr))?;
1281        self.restore_fpcr(old_fpcr)?;
1282        self.assembler.emit_fcmp(sz, f, f)?;
1283        self.assembler
1284            .emit_bcond_label(Condition::Vs, trap_badconv)?;
1285        // fallthru: trap_overflow
1286        self.emit_illegal_op_internal(TrapCode::IntegerOverflow)?;
1287
1288        self.emit_label(trap_badconv)?;
1289        self.emit_illegal_op_internal(TrapCode::BadConversionToInteger)?;
1290
1291        self.emit_label(end)?;
1292        self.restore_fpcr(old_fpcr)
1293    }
1294
1295    fn used_gprs_contains(&self, r: &GPR) -> bool {
1296        self.used_gprs & (1 << r.into_index()) != 0
1297    }
1298    fn used_simd_contains(&self, r: &NEON) -> bool {
1299        self.used_simd & (1 << r.into_index()) != 0
1300    }
1301    fn used_gprs_insert(&mut self, r: GPR) {
1302        self.used_gprs |= 1 << r.into_index();
1303    }
1304    fn used_simd_insert(&mut self, r: NEON) {
1305        self.used_simd |= 1 << r.into_index();
1306    }
1307    fn used_gprs_remove(&mut self, r: &GPR) -> bool {
1308        let ret = self.used_gprs_contains(r);
1309        self.used_gprs &= !(1 << r.into_index());
1310        ret
1311    }
1312    fn used_simd_remove(&mut self, r: &NEON) -> bool {
1313        let ret = self.used_simd_contains(r);
1314        self.used_simd &= !(1 << r.into_index());
1315        ret
1316    }
1317    fn emit_unwind_op(&mut self, op: UnwindOps<GPR, NEON>) {
1318        self.unwind_ops.push((self.get_offset().0, op));
1319    }
1320    fn emit_illegal_op_internal(&mut self, trap: TrapCode) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
1321        self.assembler.emit_udf(0xc0 | (trap as u8) as u16)
1322    }
1323}
1324
1325impl Machine for MachineARM64 {
1326    type GPR = GPR;
1327    type SIMD = NEON;
1328    fn assembler_get_offset(&self) -> Offset {
1329        self.assembler.get_offset()
1330    }
1331    fn index_from_gpr(&self, x: GPR) -> RegisterIndex {
1332        RegisterIndex(x as usize)
1333    }
1334    fn index_from_simd(&self, x: NEON) -> RegisterIndex {
1335        RegisterIndex(x as usize + 32)
1336    }
1337
1338    fn get_vmctx_reg(&self) -> GPR {
1339        GPR::X28
1340    }
1341
1342    fn get_used_gprs(&self) -> Vec<GPR> {
1343        GPR::iterator()
1344            .filter(|x| self.used_gprs & (1 << x.into_index()) != 0)
1345            .cloned()
1346            .collect()
1347    }
1348
1349    fn get_used_simd(&self) -> Vec<NEON> {
1350        NEON::iterator()
1351            .filter(|x| self.used_simd & (1 << x.into_index()) != 0)
1352            .cloned()
1353            .collect()
1354    }
1355
1356    fn pick_gpr(&self) -> Option<GPR> {
1357        use GPR::*;
1358        static REGS: &[GPR] = &[X9, X10, X11, X12, X13, X14, X15];
1359        for r in REGS {
1360            if !self.used_gprs_contains(r) {
1361                return Some(*r);
1362            }
1363        }
1364        None
1365    }
1366
1367    // Picks an unused general purpose register for internal temporary use.
1368    fn pick_temp_gpr(&self) -> Option<GPR> {
1369        use GPR::*;
1370        static REGS: &[GPR] = &[X8, X7, X6, X5, X4, X3, X2, X1];
1371        for r in REGS {
1372            if !self.used_gprs_contains(r) {
1373                return Some(*r);
1374            }
1375        }
1376        None
1377    }
1378
1379    fn acquire_temp_gpr(&mut self) -> Option<GPR> {
1380        let gpr = self.pick_temp_gpr();
1381        if let Some(x) = gpr {
1382            self.used_gprs_insert(x);
1383        }
1384        gpr
1385    }
1386
1387    fn release_gpr(&mut self, gpr: GPR) {
1388        assert!(self.used_gprs_remove(&gpr));
1389    }
1390
1391    fn reserve_unused_temp_gpr(&mut self, gpr: GPR) -> GPR {
1392        assert!(!self.used_gprs_contains(&gpr));
1393        self.used_gprs_insert(gpr);
1394        gpr
1395    }
1396
1397    fn reserve_gpr(&mut self, gpr: GPR) {
1398        self.used_gprs_insert(gpr);
1399    }
1400
1401    fn push_used_gpr(&mut self, used_gprs: &[GPR]) -> Result<usize, CompileError> {
1402        if used_gprs.len() % 2 == 1 {
1403            self.emit_push(Size::S64, Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp))?;
1404        }
1405        for r in used_gprs.iter() {
1406            self.emit_push(Size::S64, Location::GPR(*r))?;
1407        }
1408        Ok(used_gprs.len().div_ceil(2) * 16)
1409    }
1410    fn pop_used_gpr(&mut self, used_gprs: &[GPR]) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
1411        for r in used_gprs.iter().rev() {
1412            self.emit_pop(Size::S64, Location::GPR(*r))?;
1413        }
1414        if used_gprs.len() % 2 == 1 {
1415            self.emit_pop(Size::S64, Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp))?;
1416        }
1417        Ok(())
1418    }
1419
1420    // Picks an unused NEON register.
1421    fn pick_simd(&self) -> Option<NEON> {
1422        use NEON::*;
1423        static REGS: &[NEON] = &[V8, V9, V10, V11, V12];
1424        for r in REGS {
1425            if !self.used_simd_contains(r) {
1426                return Some(*r);
1427            }
1428        }
1429        None
1430    }
1431
1432    // Picks an unused NEON register for internal temporary use.
1433    fn pick_temp_simd(&self) -> Option<NEON> {
1434        use NEON::*;
1435        static REGS: &[NEON] = &[V0, V1, V2, V3, V4, V5, V6, V7];
1436        for r in REGS {
1437            if !self.used_simd_contains(r) {
1438                return Some(*r);
1439            }
1440        }
1441        None
1442    }
1443
1444    // Acquires a temporary NEON register.
1445    fn acquire_temp_simd(&mut self) -> Option<NEON> {
1446        let simd = self.pick_temp_simd();
1447        if let Some(x) = simd {
1448            self.used_simd_insert(x);
1449        }
1450        simd
1451    }
1452
1453    fn reserve_simd(&mut self, simd: NEON) {
1454        self.used_simd_insert(simd);
1455    }
1456
1457    // Releases a temporary NEON register.
1458    fn release_simd(&mut self, simd: NEON) {
1459        assert!(self.used_simd_remove(&simd));
1460    }
1461
1462    fn push_used_simd(&mut self, used_neons: &[NEON]) -> Result<usize, CompileError> {
1463        let stack_adjust = if used_neons.len() & 1 == 1 {
1464            (used_neons.len() * 8) as u32 + 8
1465        } else {
1466            (used_neons.len() * 8) as u32
1467        };
1468        self.adjust_stack(stack_adjust)?;
1469
1470        for (i, r) in used_neons.iter().enumerate() {
1471            self.assembler.emit_str(
1472                Size::S64,
1473                Location::SIMD(*r),
1474                Location::Memory(GPR::XzrSp, (i * 8) as i32),
1475            )?;
1476        }
1477        Ok(stack_adjust as usize)
1478    }
1479    fn pop_used_simd(&mut self, used_neons: &[NEON]) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
1480        for (i, r) in used_neons.iter().enumerate() {
1481            self.assembler.emit_ldr(
1482                Size::S64,
1483                Location::SIMD(*r),
1484                Location::Memory(GPR::XzrSp, (i * 8) as i32),
1485            )?;
1486        }
1487        let stack_adjust = if used_neons.len() & 1 == 1 {
1488            (used_neons.len() * 8) as u32 + 8
1489        } else {
1490            (used_neons.len() * 8) as u32
1491        };
1492        self.assembler.emit_add(
1493            Size::S64,
1494            Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp),
1495            Location::Imm32(stack_adjust as _),
1496            Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp),
1497        )
1498    }
1499
1500    /// Set the source location of the Wasm to the given offset.
1501    fn set_srcloc(&mut self, offset: u32) {
1502        self.src_loc = offset;
1503    }
1504    /// Marks each address in the code range emitted by `f` with the trap code `code`.
1505    fn mark_address_range_with_trap_code(&mut self, code: TrapCode, begin: usize, end: usize) {
1506        for i in begin..end {
1507            self.trap_table.offset_to_code.insert(i, code);
1508        }
1509        self.mark_instruction_address_end(begin);
1510    }
1511
1512    /// Marks one address as trappable with trap code `code`.
1513    fn mark_address_with_trap_code(&mut self, code: TrapCode) {
1514        let offset = self.assembler.get_offset().0;
1515        self.trap_table.offset_to_code.insert(offset, code);
1516        self.mark_instruction_address_end(offset);
1517    }
1518    /// Marks the instruction as trappable with trap code `code`. return "begin" offset
1519    fn mark_instruction_with_trap_code(&mut self, code: TrapCode) -> usize {
1520        let offset = self.assembler.get_offset().0;
1521        self.trap_table.offset_to_code.insert(offset, code);
1522        offset
1523    }
1524    /// Pushes the instruction to the address map, calculating the offset from a
1525    /// provided beginning address.
1526    fn mark_instruction_address_end(&mut self, begin: usize) {
1527        self.instructions_address_map.push(InstructionAddressMap {
1528            srcloc: SourceLoc::new(self.src_loc),
1529            code_offset: begin,
1530            code_len: self.assembler.get_offset().0 - begin,
1531        });
1532    }
1533
1534    /// Insert a StackOverflow (at offset 0)
1535    fn insert_stackoverflow(&mut self) {
1536        let offset = 0;
1537        self.trap_table
1538            .offset_to_code
1539            .insert(offset, TrapCode::StackOverflow);
1540        self.mark_instruction_address_end(offset);
1541    }
1542
1543    /// Get all current TrapInformation
1544    fn collect_trap_information(&self) -> Vec<TrapInformation> {
1545        self.trap_table
1546            .offset_to_code
1547            .clone()
1548            .into_iter()
1549            .map(|(offset, code)| TrapInformation {
1550                code_offset: offset as u32,
1551                trap_code: code,
1552            })
1553            .collect()
1554    }
1555
1556    fn instructions_address_map(&self) -> Vec<InstructionAddressMap> {
1557        self.instructions_address_map.clone()
1558    }
1559
1560    // Return a rounded stack adjustement value (must be multiple of 16bytes on ARM64 for example)
1561    fn round_stack_adjust(&self, value: usize) -> usize {
1562        if value & 0xf != 0 {
1563            ((value >> 4) + 1) << 4
1564        } else {
1565            value
1566        }
1567    }
1568
1569    // Memory location for a local on the stack
1570    fn local_on_stack(&mut self, stack_offset: i32) -> Location {
1571        Location::Memory(GPR::X29, -stack_offset)
1572    }
1573
1574    // Adjust stack for locals
1575    fn adjust_stack(&mut self, delta_stack_offset: u32) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
1576        let delta = if self.compatible_imm(delta_stack_offset as _, ImmType::Bits12) {
1577            Location::Imm32(delta_stack_offset as _)
1578        } else {
1579            let tmp = GPR::X17;
1580            self.assembler
1581                .emit_mov_imm(Location::GPR(tmp), delta_stack_offset as u64)?;
1582            Location::GPR(tmp)
1583        };
1584        self.assembler.emit_sub(
1585            Size::S64,
1586            Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp),
1587            delta,
1588            Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp),
1589        )
1590    }
1591    // restore stack
1592    fn restore_stack(&mut self, delta_stack_offset: u32) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
1593        let delta = if self.compatible_imm(delta_stack_offset as _, ImmType::Bits12) {
1594            Location::Imm32(delta_stack_offset as _)
1595        } else {
1596            let tmp = GPR::X17;
1597            self.assembler
1598                .emit_mov_imm(Location::GPR(tmp), delta_stack_offset as u64)?;
1599            Location::GPR(tmp)
1600        };
1601        self.assembler.emit_add(
1602            Size::S64,
1603            Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp),
1604            delta,
1605            Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp),
1606        )
1607    }
1608    fn pop_stack_locals(&mut self, delta_stack_offset: u32) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
1609        let real_delta = if delta_stack_offset & 15 != 0 {
1610            delta_stack_offset + 8
1611        } else {
1612            delta_stack_offset
1613        };
1614        let delta = if self.compatible_imm(real_delta as i64, ImmType::Bits12) {
1615            Location::Imm32(real_delta as _)
1616        } else {
1617            let tmp = GPR::X17;
1618            self.assembler
1619                .emit_mov_imm(Location::GPR(tmp), real_delta as u64)?;
1620            Location::GPR(tmp)
1621        };
1622        self.assembler.emit_add(
1623            Size::S64,
1624            Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp),
1625            delta,
1626            Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp),
1627        )
1628    }
1629    // push a value on the stack for a native call
1630    fn move_location_for_native(
1631        &mut self,
1632        size: Size,
1633        loc: Location,
1634        dest: Location,
1635    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
1636        match loc {
1637            Location::Imm64(_)
1638            | Location::Imm32(_)
1639            | Location::Imm8(_)
1640            | Location::Memory(_, _)
1641            | Location::Memory2(_, _, _, _) => {
1642                self.move_location(size, loc, Location::GPR(GPR::X17))?;
1643                self.move_location(size, Location::GPR(GPR::X17), dest)
1644            }
1645            _ => self.move_location(size, loc, dest),
1646        }
1647    }
1648
1649    // Zero a location that is 32bits
1650    fn zero_location(&mut self, size: Size, location: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
1651        self.move_location(size, Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp), location)
1652    }
1653
1654    // GPR Reg used for local pointer on the stack
1655    fn local_pointer(&self) -> GPR {
1656        GPR::X29
1657    }
1658
1659    // Determine whether a local should be allocated on the stack.
1660    fn is_local_on_stack(&self, idx: usize) -> bool {
1661        idx > 7
1662    }
1663
1664    // Determine a local's location.
1665    fn get_local_location(&self, idx: usize, callee_saved_regs_size: usize) -> Location {
1666        // Use callee-saved registers for the first locals.
1667        match idx {
1668            0 => Location::GPR(GPR::X19),
1669            1 => Location::GPR(GPR::X20),
1670            2 => Location::GPR(GPR::X21),
1671            3 => Location::GPR(GPR::X22),
1672            4 => Location::GPR(GPR::X23),
1673            5 => Location::GPR(GPR::X24),
1674            6 => Location::GPR(GPR::X25),
1675            7 => Location::GPR(GPR::X26),
1676            _ => Location::Memory(GPR::X29, -(((idx - 7) * 8 + callee_saved_regs_size) as i32)),
1677        }
1678    }
1679    // Move a local to the stack
1680    fn move_local(&mut self, stack_offset: i32, location: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
1681        if stack_offset < 256 {
1682            self.assembler
1683                .emit_stur(Size::S64, location, GPR::X29, -stack_offset)?;
1684        } else {
1685            let tmp = GPR::X17;
1686            if stack_offset < 0x1_0000 {
1687                self.assembler
1688                    .emit_mov_imm(Location::GPR(tmp), (-stack_offset as i64) as u64)?;
1689                self.assembler.emit_str(
1690                    Size::S64,
1691                    location,
1692                    Location::Memory2(GPR::X29, tmp, Multiplier::One, 0),
1693                )?;
1694            } else {
1695                self.assembler
1696                    .emit_mov_imm(Location::GPR(tmp), (stack_offset as i64) as u64)?;
1697                self.assembler.emit_sub(
1698                    Size::S64,
1699                    Location::GPR(GPR::X29),
1700                    Location::GPR(tmp),
1701                    Location::GPR(tmp),
1702                )?;
1703                self.assembler
1704                    .emit_str(Size::S64, location, Location::GPR(tmp))?;
1705            }
1706        }
1707        match location {
1708            Location::GPR(x) => self.emit_unwind_op(UnwindOps::SaveRegister {
1709                reg: UnwindRegister::<GPR, NEON>::GPR(x),
1710                bp_neg_offset: stack_offset,
1711            }),
1712            Location::SIMD(x) => self.emit_unwind_op(UnwindOps::SaveRegister {
1713                reg: UnwindRegister::FPR(x),
1714                bp_neg_offset: stack_offset,
1715            }),
1716            _ => (),
1717        }
1718        Ok(())
1719    }
1720
1721    // List of register to save, depending on the CallingConvention
1722    fn list_to_save(&self, _calling_convention: CallingConvention) -> Vec<Location> {
1723        vec![]
1724    }
1725
1726    // Get param location, MUST be called in order!
1727    fn get_param_location(
1728        &self,
1729        idx: usize,
1730        sz: Size,
1731        stack_args: &mut usize,
1732        calling_convention: CallingConvention,
1733    ) -> Location {
1734        match calling_convention {
1735            CallingConvention::AppleAarch64 => match idx {
1736                0 => Location::GPR(GPR::X0),
1737                1 => Location::GPR(GPR::X1),
1738                2 => Location::GPR(GPR::X2),
1739                3 => Location::GPR(GPR::X3),
1740                4 => Location::GPR(GPR::X4),
1741                5 => Location::GPR(GPR::X5),
1742                6 => Location::GPR(GPR::X6),
1743                7 => Location::GPR(GPR::X7),
1744                _ => {
1745                    let sz = 1
1746                        << match sz {
1747                            Size::S8 => 0,
1748                            Size::S16 => 1,
1749                            Size::S32 => 2,
1750                            Size::S64 => 3,
1751                        };
1752                    // align first
1753                    if sz > 1 && *stack_args & (sz - 1) != 0 {
1754                        *stack_args = (*stack_args + (sz - 1)) & !(sz - 1);
1755                    }
1756                    let loc = Location::Memory(GPR::XzrSp, *stack_args as i32);
1757                    *stack_args += sz;
1758                    loc
1759                }
1760            },
1761            _ => match idx {
1762                0 => Location::GPR(GPR::X0),
1763                1 => Location::GPR(GPR::X1),
1764                2 => Location::GPR(GPR::X2),
1765                3 => Location::GPR(GPR::X3),
1766                4 => Location::GPR(GPR::X4),
1767                5 => Location::GPR(GPR::X5),
1768                6 => Location::GPR(GPR::X6),
1769                7 => Location::GPR(GPR::X7),
1770                _ => {
1771                    let loc = Location::Memory(GPR::XzrSp, *stack_args as i32);
1772                    *stack_args += 8;
1773                    loc
1774                }
1775            },
1776        }
1777    }
1778    // Get call param location, MUST be called in order!
1779    fn get_call_param_location(
1780        &self,
1781        idx: usize,
1782        sz: Size,
1783        stack_args: &mut usize,
1784        calling_convention: CallingConvention,
1785    ) -> Location {
1786        match calling_convention {
1787            CallingConvention::AppleAarch64 => match idx {
1788                0 => Location::GPR(GPR::X0),
1789                1 => Location::GPR(GPR::X1),
1790                2 => Location::GPR(GPR::X2),
1791                3 => Location::GPR(GPR::X3),
1792                4 => Location::GPR(GPR::X4),
1793                5 => Location::GPR(GPR::X5),
1794                6 => Location::GPR(GPR::X6),
1795                7 => Location::GPR(GPR::X7),
1796                _ => {
1797                    let sz = 1
1798                        << match sz {
1799                            Size::S8 => 0,
1800                            Size::S16 => 1,
1801                            Size::S32 => 2,
1802                            Size::S64 => 3,
1803                        };
1804                    // align first
1805                    if sz > 1 && *stack_args & (sz - 1) != 0 {
1806                        *stack_args = (*stack_args + (sz - 1)) & !(sz - 1);
1807                    }
1808                    let loc = Location::Memory(GPR::X29, 16 * 2 + *stack_args as i32);
1809                    *stack_args += sz;
1810                    loc
1811                }
1812            },
1813            _ => match idx {
1814                0 => Location::GPR(GPR::X0),
1815                1 => Location::GPR(GPR::X1),
1816                2 => Location::GPR(GPR::X2),
1817                3 => Location::GPR(GPR::X3),
1818                4 => Location::GPR(GPR::X4),
1819                5 => Location::GPR(GPR::X5),
1820                6 => Location::GPR(GPR::X6),
1821                7 => Location::GPR(GPR::X7),
1822                _ => {
1823                    let loc = Location::Memory(GPR::X29, 16 * 2 + *stack_args as i32);
1824                    *stack_args += 8;
1825                    loc
1826                }
1827            },
1828        }
1829    }
1830    // Get simple param location, Will not be accurate for Apple calling convention on "stack" arguments
1831    fn get_simple_param_location(
1832        &self,
1833        idx: usize,
1834        calling_convention: CallingConvention,
1835    ) -> Location {
1836        #[allow(clippy::match_single_binding)]
1837        match calling_convention {
1838            _ => match idx {
1839                0 => Location::GPR(GPR::X0),
1840                1 => Location::GPR(GPR::X1),
1841                2 => Location::GPR(GPR::X2),
1842                3 => Location::GPR(GPR::X3),
1843                4 => Location::GPR(GPR::X4),
1844                5 => Location::GPR(GPR::X5),
1845                6 => Location::GPR(GPR::X6),
1846                7 => Location::GPR(GPR::X7),
1847                _ => Location::Memory(GPR::X29, (16 * 2 + (idx - 8) * 8) as i32),
1848            },
1849        }
1850    }
1851    // move a location to another
1852    fn move_location(
1853        &mut self,
1854        size: Size,
1855        source: Location,
1856        dest: Location,
1857    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
1858        match source {
1859            Location::GPR(_) | Location::SIMD(_) => match dest {
1860                Location::GPR(_) | Location::SIMD(_) => self.assembler.emit_mov(size, source, dest),
1861                Location::Memory(addr, offs) => {
1862                    if self.offset_is_ok(size, offs) {
1863                        self.assembler.emit_str(size, source, dest)
1864                    } else if self.compatible_imm(offs as i64, ImmType::UnscaledOffset) {
1865                        self.assembler.emit_stur(size, source, addr, offs)
1866                    } else {
1867                        let tmp = GPR::X17;
1868                        if offs < 0 {
1869                            self.assembler
1870                                .emit_mov_imm(Location::GPR(tmp), (-offs) as u64)?;
1871                            self.assembler.emit_sub(
1872                                Size::S64,
1873                                Location::GPR(addr),
1874                                Location::GPR(tmp),
1875                                Location::GPR(tmp),
1876                            )?;
1877                        } else {
1878                            self.assembler
1879                                .emit_mov_imm(Location::GPR(tmp), offs as u64)?;
1880                            self.assembler.emit_add(
1881                                Size::S64,
1882                                Location::GPR(addr),
1883                                Location::GPR(tmp),
1884                                Location::GPR(tmp),
1885                            )?;
1886                        }
1887                        self.assembler
1888                            .emit_str(size, source, Location::Memory(tmp, 0))
1889                    }
1890                }
1891                _ => codegen_error!(
1892                    "singlepass can't emit move_location {:?} {:?} => {:?}",
1893                    size,
1894                    source,
1895                    dest
1896                ),
1897            },
1898            Location::Imm8(_) => match dest {
1899                Location::GPR(_) => self.assembler.emit_mov(size, source, dest),
1900                Location::Memory(_, _) => match size {
1901                    Size::S64 => self.emit_relaxed_str64(source, dest),
1902                    Size::S32 => self.emit_relaxed_str32(source, dest),
1903                    Size::S16 => self.emit_relaxed_str16(source, dest),
1904                    Size::S8 => self.emit_relaxed_str8(source, dest),
1905                },
1906                _ => codegen_error!(
1907                    "singlepass can't emit move_location {:?} {:?} => {:?}",
1908                    size,
1909                    source,
1910                    dest
1911                ),
1912            },
1913            Location::Imm32(val) => match dest {
1914                Location::GPR(_) => self.assembler.emit_mov_imm(dest, val as u64),
1915                Location::Memory(_, _) => match size {
1916                    Size::S64 => self.emit_relaxed_str64(source, dest),
1917                    Size::S32 => self.emit_relaxed_str32(source, dest),
1918                    Size::S16 => self.emit_relaxed_str16(source, dest),
1919                    Size::S8 => self.emit_relaxed_str8(source, dest),
1920                },
1921                _ => codegen_error!(
1922                    "singlepass can't emit move_location {:?} {:?} => {:?}",
1923                    size,
1924                    source,
1925                    dest
1926                ),
1927            },
1928            Location::Imm64(val) => match dest {
1929                Location::GPR(_) => self.assembler.emit_mov_imm(dest, val),
1930                Location::Memory(_, _) => match size {
1931                    Size::S64 => self.emit_relaxed_str64(source, dest),
1932                    Size::S32 => self.emit_relaxed_str32(source, dest),
1933                    Size::S16 => self.emit_relaxed_str16(source, dest),
1934                    Size::S8 => self.emit_relaxed_str8(source, dest),
1935                },
1936                _ => codegen_error!(
1937                    "singlepass can't emit move_location {:?} {:?} => {:?}",
1938                    size,
1939                    source,
1940                    dest
1941                ),
1942            },
1943            Location::Memory(addr, offs) => match dest {
1944                Location::GPR(_) | Location::SIMD(_) => {
1945                    if self.offset_is_ok(size, offs) {
1946                        self.assembler.emit_ldr(size, dest, source)
1947                    } else if offs > -256 && offs < 256 {
1948                        self.assembler.emit_ldur(size, dest, addr, offs)
1949                    } else {
1950                        let tmp = GPR::X17;
1951                        if offs < 0 {
1952                            self.assembler
1953                                .emit_mov_imm(Location::GPR(tmp), (-offs) as u64)?;
1954                            self.assembler.emit_sub(
1955                                Size::S64,
1956                                Location::GPR(addr),
1957                                Location::GPR(tmp),
1958                                Location::GPR(tmp),
1959                            )?;
1960                        } else {
1961                            self.assembler
1962                                .emit_mov_imm(Location::GPR(tmp), offs as u64)?;
1963                            self.assembler.emit_add(
1964                                Size::S64,
1965                                Location::GPR(addr),
1966                                Location::GPR(tmp),
1967                                Location::GPR(tmp),
1968                            )?;
1969                        }
1970                        self.assembler
1971                            .emit_ldr(size, dest, Location::Memory(tmp, 0))
1972                    }
1973                }
1974                _ => {
1975                    let mut temps = vec![];
1976                    let src =
1977                        self.location_to_reg(size, source, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
1978                    self.move_location(size, src, dest)?;
1979                    for r in temps {
1980                        self.release_gpr(r);
1981                    }
1982                    Ok(())
1983                }
1984            },
1985            _ => codegen_error!(
1986                "singlepass can't emit move_location {:?} {:?} => {:?}",
1987                size,
1988                source,
1989                dest
1990            ),
1991        }
1992    }
1993    // move a location to another
1994    fn move_location_extend(
1995        &mut self,
1996        size_val: Size,
1997        signed: bool,
1998        source: Location,
1999        size_op: Size,
2000        dest: Location,
2001    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2002        if size_op != Size::S64 {
2003            codegen_error!("singlepass move_location_extend unreachable");
2004        }
2005        let mut temps = vec![];
2006        let dst = self.location_to_reg(size_op, dest, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
2007        let src = match (size_val, signed, source) {
2008            (Size::S64, _, _) => source,
2009            (Size::S32, false, Location::GPR(_)) => {
2010                self.assembler.emit_mov(size_val, source, dst)?;
2011                dst
2012            }
2013            (Size::S8, false, Location::GPR(_)) => {
2014                self.assembler.emit_uxtb(size_op, source, dst)?;
2015                dst
2016            }
2017            (Size::S16, false, Location::GPR(_)) => {
2018                self.assembler.emit_uxth(size_op, source, dst)?;
2019                dst
2020            }
2021            (Size::S8, true, Location::GPR(_)) => {
2022                self.assembler.emit_sxtb(size_op, source, dst)?;
2023                dst
2024            }
2025            (Size::S16, true, Location::GPR(_)) => {
2026                self.assembler.emit_sxth(size_op, source, dst)?;
2027                dst
2028            }
2029            (Size::S32, true, Location::GPR(_)) => {
2030                self.assembler.emit_sxtw(size_op, source, dst)?;
2031                dst
2032            }
2033            (Size::S32, false, Location::Memory(_, _)) => {
2034                self.emit_relaxed_ldr32(size_op, dst, source)?;
2035                dst
2036            }
2037            (Size::S32, true, Location::Memory(_, _)) => {
2038                self.emit_relaxed_ldr32s(size_op, dst, source)?;
2039                dst
2040            }
2041            (Size::S16, false, Location::Memory(_, _)) => {
2042                self.emit_relaxed_ldr16(size_op, dst, source)?;
2043                dst
2044            }
2045            (Size::S16, true, Location::Memory(_, _)) => {
2046                self.emit_relaxed_ldr16s(size_op, dst, source)?;
2047                dst
2048            }
2049            (Size::S8, false, Location::Memory(_, _)) => {
2050                self.emit_relaxed_ldr8(size_op, dst, source)?;
2051                dst
2052            }
2053            (Size::S8, true, Location::Memory(_, _)) => {
2054                self.emit_relaxed_ldr8s(size_op, dst, source)?;
2055                dst
2056            }
2057            _ => codegen_error!(
2058                "singlepass can't emit move_location_extend {:?} {:?} {:?} => {:?} {:?}",
2059                size_val,
2060                signed,
2061                source,
2062                size_op,
2063                dest
2064            ),
2065        };
2066        if src != dst {
2067            self.move_location(size_op, src, dst)?;
2068        }
2069        if dst != dest {
2070            self.move_location(size_op, dst, dest)?;
2071        }
2072        for r in temps {
2073            self.release_gpr(r);
2074        }
2075        Ok(())
2076    }
2077
2078    // Init the stack loc counter
2079    fn init_stack_loc(
2080        &mut self,
2081        init_stack_loc_cnt: u64,
2082        last_stack_loc: Location,
2083    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2084        let label = self.assembler.get_label();
2085        let mut temps = vec![];
2086        let dest = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
2087            CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
2088        })?;
2089        temps.push(dest);
2090        let cnt = self.location_to_reg(
2091            Size::S64,
2092            Location::Imm64(init_stack_loc_cnt),
2093            &mut temps,
2094            ImmType::None,
2095            true,
2096            None,
2097        )?;
2098        let dest = match last_stack_loc {
2099            Location::GPR(_) => codegen_error!("singlepass init_stack_loc unreachable"),
2100            Location::SIMD(_) => codegen_error!("singlepass init_stack_loc unreachable"),
2101            Location::Memory(reg, offset) => {
2102                if offset < 0 {
2103                    let offset = (-offset) as u32;
2104                    if self.compatible_imm(offset as i64, ImmType::Bits12) {
2105                        self.assembler.emit_sub(
2106                            Size::S64,
2107                            Location::GPR(reg),
2108                            Location::Imm32(offset),
2109                            Location::GPR(dest),
2110                        )?;
2111                    } else {
2112                        let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
2113                            CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
2114                        })?;
2115                        self.assembler
2116                            .emit_mov_imm(Location::GPR(tmp), (offset as i64) as u64)?;
2117                        self.assembler.emit_sub(
2118                            Size::S64,
2119                            Location::GPR(reg),
2120                            Location::GPR(tmp),
2121                            Location::GPR(dest),
2122                        )?;
2123                        temps.push(tmp);
2124                    }
2125                    dest
2126                } else {
2127                    let offset = offset as u32;
2128                    if self.compatible_imm(offset as i64, ImmType::Bits12) {
2129                        self.assembler.emit_add(
2130                            Size::S64,
2131                            Location::GPR(reg),
2132                            Location::Imm32(offset),
2133                            Location::GPR(dest),
2134                        )?;
2135                    } else {
2136                        let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
2137                            CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
2138                        })?;
2139                        self.assembler
2140                            .emit_mov_imm(Location::GPR(tmp), (offset as i64) as u64)?;
2141                        self.assembler.emit_add(
2142                            Size::S64,
2143                            Location::GPR(reg),
2144                            Location::GPR(tmp),
2145                            Location::GPR(dest),
2146                        )?;
2147                        temps.push(tmp);
2148                    }
2149                    dest
2150                }
2151            }
2152            _ => codegen_error!("singlepass can't emit init_stack_loc {:?}", last_stack_loc),
2153        };
2154        self.assembler.emit_label(label)?;
2155        self.assembler
2156            .emit_stria(Size::S64, Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp), dest, 8)?;
2157        self.assembler
2158            .emit_sub(Size::S64, cnt, Location::Imm8(1), cnt)?;
2159        self.assembler.emit_cbnz_label(Size::S64, cnt, label)?;
2160        for r in temps {
2161            self.release_gpr(r);
2162        }
2163        Ok(())
2164    }
2165    // Restore save_area
2166    fn restore_saved_area(&mut self, saved_area_offset: i32) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2167        let real_delta = if saved_area_offset & 15 != 0 {
2168            self.pushed = true;
2169            saved_area_offset + 8
2170        } else {
2171            self.pushed = false;
2172            saved_area_offset
2173        };
2174        if self.compatible_imm(real_delta as _, ImmType::Bits12) {
2175            self.assembler.emit_sub(
2176                Size::S64,
2177                Location::GPR(GPR::X29),
2178                Location::Imm32(real_delta as _),
2179                Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp),
2180            )?;
2181        } else {
2182            let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
2183                CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
2184            })?;
2185            self.assembler
2186                .emit_mov_imm(Location::GPR(tmp), real_delta as u64)?;
2187            self.assembler.emit_sub(
2188                Size::S64,
2189                Location::GPR(GPR::X29),
2190                Location::GPR(tmp),
2191                Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp),
2192            )?;
2193            self.release_gpr(tmp);
2194        }
2195        Ok(())
2196    }
2197    // Pop a location
2198    fn pop_location(&mut self, location: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2199        self.emit_pop(Size::S64, location)
2200    }
2201    // Create a new `MachineState` with default values.
2202    fn new_machine_state(&self) -> MachineState {
2203        new_machine_state()
2204    }

2206    // assembler finalize
2207    fn assembler_finalize(self) -> Result<Vec<u8>, CompileError> {
2208        self.assembler.finalize().map_err(|e| {
2209            CompileError::Codegen(format!("Assembler failed finalization with: {e:?}"))
2210        })
2211    }

2213    fn get_offset(&self) -> Offset {
2214        self.assembler.get_offset()
2215    }
2216
2217    fn finalize_function(&mut self) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2218        self.assembler.finalize_function();
2219        Ok(())
2220    }
2221
2222    fn emit_function_prolog(&mut self) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2223        self.emit_double_push(Size::S64, Location::GPR(GPR::X29), Location::GPR(GPR::X30))?; // save LR too
2224        self.emit_unwind_op(UnwindOps::Push2Regs {
2225            reg1: UnwindRegister::GPR(GPR::X29),
2226            reg2: UnwindRegister::GPR(GPR::X30),
2227            up_to_sp: 16,
2228        });
2229        self.emit_double_push(Size::S64, Location::GPR(GPR::X27), Location::GPR(GPR::X28))?;
2230        self.emit_unwind_op(UnwindOps::Push2Regs {
2231            reg1: UnwindRegister::GPR(GPR::X27),
2232            reg2: UnwindRegister::GPR(GPR::X28),
2233            up_to_sp: 32,
2234        });
2235        // cannot use mov, because XSP is XZR there. Need to use ADD with #0
2236        self.assembler.emit_add(
2237            Size::S64,
2238            Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp),
2239            Location::Imm8(0),
2240            Location::GPR(GPR::X29),
2241        )?;
2242        self.emit_unwind_op(UnwindOps::DefineNewFrame);
2243        Ok(())
2244    }
2245
2246    fn emit_function_epilog(&mut self) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2247        // cannot use mov, because XSP is XZR there. Need to use ADD with #0
2248        self.assembler.emit_add(
2249            Size::S64,
2250            Location::GPR(GPR::X29),
2251            Location::Imm8(0),
2252            Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp),
2253        )?;
2254        self.pushed = false; // SP is restored, consider it aligned
2255        self.emit_double_pop(Size::S64, Location::GPR(GPR::X27), Location::GPR(GPR::X28))?;
2256        self.emit_double_pop(Size::S64, Location::GPR(GPR::X29), Location::GPR(GPR::X30))?;
2257        Ok(())
2258    }
2259
2260    fn emit_function_return_value(
2261        &mut self,
2262        ty: WpType,
2263        canonicalize: bool,
2264        loc: Location,
2265    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2266        if canonicalize {
2267            self.canonicalize_nan(
2268                match ty {
2269                    WpType::F32 => Size::S32,
2270                    WpType::F64 => Size::S64,
2271                    _ => unreachable!(),
2272                },
2273                loc,
2274                Location::GPR(GPR::X0),
2275            )?;
2276        } else {
2277            self.emit_relaxed_mov(Size::S64, loc, Location::GPR(GPR::X0))?;
2278        }
2279        Ok(())
2280    }
2281
2282    fn emit_function_return_float(&mut self) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2283        self.assembler
2284            .emit_mov(Size::S64, Location::GPR(GPR::X0), Location::SIMD(NEON::V0))
2285    }
2286
2287    fn arch_supports_canonicalize_nan(&self) -> bool {
2288        self.assembler.arch_supports_canonicalize_nan()
2289    }
2290    fn canonicalize_nan(
2291        &mut self,
2292        sz: Size,
2293        input: Location,
2294        output: Location,
2295    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2296        let mut tempn = vec![];
2297        let mut temps = vec![];
2298        let old_fpcr = self.set_default_nan(&mut temps)?;
2299        // use FMAX (input, intput) => output to automaticaly normalize the NaN
2300        match (sz, input, output) {
2301            (Size::S32, Location::SIMD(_), Location::SIMD(_)) => {
2302                self.assembler.emit_fmax(sz, input, input, output)?;
2303            }
2304            (Size::S64, Location::SIMD(_), Location::SIMD(_)) => {
2305                self.assembler.emit_fmax(sz, input, input, output)?;
2306            }
2307            (Size::S32, Location::SIMD(_), _) | (Size::S64, Location::SIMD(_), _) => {
2308                let tmp = self.location_to_neon(sz, output, &mut tempn, ImmType::None, false)?;
2309                self.assembler.emit_fmax(sz, input, input, tmp)?;
2310                self.move_location(sz, tmp, output)?;
2311            }
2312            (Size::S32, Location::Memory(_, _), _) | (Size::S64, Location::Memory(_, _), _) => {
2313                let src = self.location_to_neon(sz, input, &mut tempn, ImmType::None, true)?;
2314                let tmp = self.location_to_neon(sz, output, &mut tempn, ImmType::None, false)?;
2315                self.assembler.emit_fmax(sz, src, src, tmp)?;
2316                if tmp != output {
2317                    self.move_location(sz, tmp, output)?;
2318                }
2319            }
2320            _ => codegen_error!(
2321                "singlepass can't emit canonicalize_nan {:?} {:?} {:?}",
2322                sz,
2323                input,
2324                output
2325            ),
2326        }
2327
2328        self.restore_fpcr(old_fpcr)?;
2329        for r in temps {
2330            self.release_gpr(r);
2331        }
2332        for r in tempn {
2333            self.release_simd(r);
2334        }
2335        Ok(())
2336    }
2337
2338    fn emit_illegal_op(&mut self, trap: TrapCode) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2339        let offset = self.assembler.get_offset().0;
2340        self.assembler.emit_udf(0xc0 | (trap as u8) as u16)?;
2341        self.mark_instruction_address_end(offset);
2342        Ok(())
2343    }

2347    fn emit_label(&mut self, label: Label) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2348        self.assembler.emit_label(label)
2349    }

2354        self.assembler.emit_call_register(reg)

2358    }
2359    fn get_gpr_for_ret(&self) -> GPR {
2360        GPR::X0
2361    }
2362    fn get_simd_for_ret(&self) -> NEON {
2363        NEON::V0
2364    }

2366    fn arch_requires_indirect_call_trampoline(&self) -> bool {

2369
2370    fn arch_emit_indirect_call_with_trampoline(
2371        &mut self,
2372        location: Location,
2373    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2374        self.assembler
2375            .arch_emit_indirect_call_with_trampoline(location)
2376    }
2377
2378    fn emit_debug_breakpoint(&mut self) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2379        self.assembler.emit_brk()
2380    }
2381
2382    fn emit_call_location(&mut self, location: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2383        let mut temps = vec![];
2384        let loc = self.location_to_reg(
2385            Size::S64,
2386            location,
2387            &mut temps,
2388            ImmType::None,
2389            true,
2390            Some(GPR::X27),
2391        )?;
2392        match loc {
2393            Location::GPR(reg) => self.assembler.emit_call_register(reg),
2394            _ => codegen_error!("singlepass can't emit CALL Location"),
2395        }?;
2396        for r in temps {
2397            self.release_gpr(r);
2398        }
2399        Ok(())
2400    }
2401    // math
2402    fn location_add(
2403        &mut self,
2404        size: Size,
2405        source: Location,
2406        dest: Location,
2407        flags: bool,
2408    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2409        let mut temps = vec![];
2410        let src = self.location_to_reg(size, source, &mut temps, ImmType::Bits12, true, None)?;
2411        let dst = self.location_to_reg(size, dest, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
2412        if flags {
2413            self.assembler.emit_adds(size, dst, src, dst)?;
2414        } else {
2415            self.assembler.emit_add(size, dst, src, dst)?;
2416        }
2417        if dst != dest {
2418            self.move_location(size, dst, dest)?;
2419        }
2420        for r in temps {
2421            self.release_gpr(r);
2422        }
2423        Ok(())
2424    }
2425    fn location_cmp(
2426        &mut self,
2427        size: Size,
2428        source: Location,
2429        dest: Location,
2430    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2431        self.emit_relaxed_binop(Assembler::emit_cmp, size, source, dest, false)
2432    }
2433    fn jmp_unconditional(&mut self, label: Label) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2434        self.assembler.emit_b_label(label)
2435    }
2436
2437    fn jmp_on_condition(
2438        &mut self,
2439        cond: UnsignedCondition,
2440        size: Size,
2441        loc_a: AbstractLocation<Self::GPR, Self::SIMD>,
2442        loc_b: AbstractLocation<Self::GPR, Self::SIMD>,
2443        label: Label,
2444    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2445        self.emit_relaxed_binop(Assembler::emit_cmp, size, loc_b, loc_a, false)?;
2446        let cond = match cond {
2447            UnsignedCondition::Equal => Condition::Eq,
2448            UnsignedCondition::NotEqual => Condition::Ne,
2449            UnsignedCondition::Above => Condition::Hi,
2450            UnsignedCondition::AboveEqual => Condition::Cs,
2451            UnsignedCondition::Below => Condition::Cc,
2452            UnsignedCondition::BelowEqual => Condition::Ls,
2453        };
2454        self.assembler.emit_bcond_label_far(cond, label)
2455    }
2456
2457    // jmp table
2458    fn emit_jmp_to_jumptable(&mut self, label: Label, cond: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2459        let tmp1 = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
2460            CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
2461        })?;
2462        let tmp2 = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
2463            CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
2464        })?;
2465
2466        self.assembler.emit_load_label(tmp1, label)?;
2467        self.move_location(Size::S32, cond, Location::GPR(tmp2))?;
2468
2469        self.assembler.emit_add_lsl(
2470            Size::S64,
2471            Location::GPR(tmp1),
2472            Location::GPR(tmp2),
2473            2,
2474            Location::GPR(tmp2),
2475        )?;
2476        self.assembler.emit_b_register(tmp2)?;
2477        self.release_gpr(tmp2);
2478        self.release_gpr(tmp1);
2479        Ok(())
2480    }
2481
2482    fn align_for_loop(&mut self) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2483        // noting to do on ARM64
2484        Ok(())
2485    }
2486
2487    fn emit_ret(&mut self) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2488        self.assembler.emit_ret()
2489    }
2490
2491    fn emit_push(&mut self, size: Size, loc: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2492        self.emit_push(size, loc)
2493    }
2494    fn emit_pop(&mut self, size: Size, loc: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2495        self.emit_pop(size, loc)
2496    }
2497
2498    fn emit_memory_fence(&mut self) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2499        self.assembler.emit_dmb()
2500    }
2501
2502    fn emit_imul_imm32(&mut self, size: Size, imm32: u32, gpr: GPR) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2503        let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
2504            CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
2505        })?;
2506        self.assembler
2507            .emit_mov_imm(Location::GPR(tmp), imm32 as u64)?;
2508        self.assembler.emit_mul(
2509            size,
2510            Location::GPR(gpr),
2511            Location::GPR(tmp),
2512            Location::GPR(gpr),
2513        )?;
2514        self.release_gpr(tmp);
2515        Ok(())
2516    }
2517
2518    // relaxed binop based...
2519    fn emit_relaxed_mov(
2520        &mut self,
2521        sz: Size,
2522        src: Location,
2523        dst: Location,
2524    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2525        self.emit_relaxed_binop(Assembler::emit_mov, sz, src, dst, true)
2526    }
2527    fn emit_relaxed_cmp(
2528        &mut self,
2529        sz: Size,
2530        src: Location,
2531        dst: Location,
2532    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2533        self.emit_relaxed_binop(Assembler::emit_cmp, sz, src, dst, false)
2534    }
2535    fn emit_relaxed_sign_extension(
2536        &mut self,
2537        sz_src: Size,
2538        src: Location,
2539        sz_dst: Size,
2540        dst: Location,
2541    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2542        match (src, dst) {
2543            (Location::Memory(_, _), Location::GPR(_)) => match sz_src {
2544                Size::S8 => self.emit_relaxed_ldr8s(sz_dst, dst, src),
2545                Size::S16 => self.emit_relaxed_ldr16s(sz_dst, dst, src),
2546                Size::S32 => self.emit_relaxed_ldr32s(sz_dst, dst, src),
2547                _ => codegen_error!("singlepass emit_relaxed_sign_extension unreachable"),
2548            },
2549            _ => {
2550                let mut temps = vec![];
2551                let src =
2552                    self.location_to_reg(sz_src, src, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
2553                let dest =
2554                    self.location_to_reg(sz_dst, dst, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
2555                match sz_src {
2556                    Size::S8 => self.assembler.emit_sxtb(sz_dst, src, dest),
2557                    Size::S16 => self.assembler.emit_sxth(sz_dst, src, dest),
2558                    Size::S32 => self.assembler.emit_sxtw(sz_dst, src, dest),
2559                    _ => codegen_error!("singlepass emit_relaxed_sign_extension unreachable"),
2560                }?;
2561                if dst != dest {
2562                    self.move_location(sz_dst, dest, dst)?;
2563                }
2564                for r in temps {
2565                    self.release_gpr(r);
2566                }
2567                Ok(())
2568            }
2569        }
2570    }
2571

2602    fn emit_binop_mul32(
2603        &mut self,
2604        loc_a: Location,
2605        loc_b: Location,
2606        ret: Location,
2607    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {

2609            Assembler::emit_mul,

2612            loc_b,
2613            ret,
2614            ImmType::None,

2617    fn emit_binop_udiv32(
2618        &mut self,
2619        loc_a: Location,
2620        loc_b: Location,
2621        ret: Location,
2622        integer_division_by_zero: Label,
2623    ) -> Result<usize, CompileError> {
2624        let mut temps = vec![];
2625        let src1 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, loc_a, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
2626        let src2 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, loc_b, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
2627        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
2628
2629        self.assembler
2630            .emit_cbz_label_far(Size::S32, src2, integer_division_by_zero)?;
2631        let offset = self.mark_instruction_with_trap_code(TrapCode::IntegerOverflow);
2632        self.assembler.emit_udiv(Size::S32, src1, src2, dest)?;
2633        if ret != dest {
2634            self.move_location(Size::S32, dest, ret)?;
2635        }
2636        for r in temps {
2637            self.release_gpr(r);
2638        }
2639        Ok(offset)
2640    }
2641    fn emit_binop_sdiv32(
2642        &mut self,
2643        loc_a: Location,
2644        loc_b: Location,
2645        ret: Location,
2646        integer_division_by_zero: Label,
2647        integer_overflow: Label,
2648    ) -> Result<usize, CompileError> {
2649        let mut temps = vec![];
2650        let src1 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, loc_a, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
2651        let src2 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, loc_b, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
2652        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
2653
2654        self.assembler
2655            .emit_cbz_label_far(Size::S32, src2, integer_division_by_zero)?;
2656        let label_nooverflow = self.assembler.get_label();
2657        let tmp = self.location_to_reg(
2658            Size::S32,
2659            Location::Imm32(0x80000000),
2660            &mut temps,
2661            ImmType::None,
2662            true,
2663            None,
2664        )?;
2665        self.assembler.emit_cmp(Size::S32, tmp, src1)?;
2666        self.assembler
2667            .emit_bcond_label(Condition::Ne, label_nooverflow)?;
2668        self.assembler.emit_movn(Size::S32, tmp, 0)?;
2669        self.assembler.emit_cmp(Size::S32, tmp, src2)?;
2670        self.assembler
2671            .emit_bcond_label_far(Condition::Eq, integer_overflow)?;
2672        let offset = self.mark_instruction_with_trap_code(TrapCode::IntegerOverflow);
2673        self.assembler.emit_label(label_nooverflow)?;
2674        self.assembler.emit_sdiv(Size::S32, src1, src2, dest)?;
2675        if ret != dest {
2676            self.move_location(Size::S32, dest, ret)?;
2677        }
2678        for r in temps {
2679            self.release_gpr(r);
2680        }
2681        Ok(offset)
2682    }
2683    fn emit_binop_urem32(
2684        &mut self,
2685        loc_a: Location,
2686        loc_b: Location,
2687        ret: Location,
2688        integer_division_by_zero: Label,
2689    ) -> Result<usize, CompileError> {
2690        let mut temps = vec![];
2691        let src1 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, loc_a, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
2692        let src2 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, loc_b, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
2693        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
2694        let dest = if dest == src1 || dest == src2 {
2695            let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
2696                CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
2697            })?;
2698            temps.push(tmp);
2699            self.assembler
2700                .emit_mov(Size::S32, dest, Location::GPR(tmp))?;
2701            Location::GPR(tmp)
2702        } else {
2703            dest
2704        };
2705        self.assembler
2706            .emit_cbz_label_far(Size::S32, src2, integer_division_by_zero)?;
2707        let offset = self.mark_instruction_with_trap_code(TrapCode::IntegerOverflow);
2708        self.assembler.emit_udiv(Size::S32, src1, src2, dest)?;
2709        // unsigned remainder : src1 - (src1/src2)*src2
2710        self.assembler
2711            .emit_msub(Size::S32, dest, src2, src1, dest)?;
2712        if ret != dest {
2713            self.move_location(Size::S32, dest, ret)?;
2714        }
2715        for r in temps {
2716            self.release_gpr(r);
2717        }
2718        Ok(offset)
2719    }
2720    fn emit_binop_srem32(
2721        &mut self,
2722        loc_a: Location,
2723        loc_b: Location,
2724        ret: Location,
2725        integer_division_by_zero: Label,
2726    ) -> Result<usize, CompileError> {
2727        let mut temps = vec![];
2728        let src1 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, loc_a, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
2729        let src2 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, loc_b, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
2730        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
2731        let dest = if dest == src1 || dest == src2 {
2732            let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
2733                CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
2734            })?;
2735            temps.push(tmp);
2736            self.assembler
2737                .emit_mov(Size::S32, dest, Location::GPR(tmp))?;
2738            Location::GPR(tmp)
2739        } else {
2740            dest
2741        };
2742        self.assembler
2743            .emit_cbz_label_far(Size::S32, src2, integer_division_by_zero)?;
2744        let offset = self.mark_instruction_with_trap_code(TrapCode::IntegerOverflow);
2745        self.assembler.emit_sdiv(Size::S32, src1, src2, dest)?;
2746        // unsigned remainder : src1 - (src1/src2)*src2
2747        self.assembler
2748            .emit_msub(Size::S32, dest, src2, src1, dest)?;
2749        if ret != dest {
2750            self.move_location(Size::S32, dest, ret)?;
2751        }
2752        for r in temps {
2753            self.release_gpr(r);
2754        }
2755        Ok(offset)
2756    }

2882    fn i32_clz(&mut self, src: Location, dst: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
