2885    fn i32_ctz(&mut self, src: Location, dst: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2886        let mut temps = vec![];
2887        let src = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, src, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
2888        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, dst, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
2889        self.assembler.emit_rbit(Size::S32, src, dest)?;
2890        self.assembler.emit_clz(Size::S32, dest, dest)?;
2891        if dst != dest {
2892            self.move_location(Size::S32, dest, dst)?;
2893        }
2894        for r in temps {
2895            self.release_gpr(r);
2896        }
2897        Ok(())
2898    }
2899    fn i32_popcnt(&mut self, loc: Location, ret: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2900        if self.has_neon {
2901            let mut temps = vec![];
2902
2903            let src_gpr =
2904                self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, loc, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
2905            let dst_gpr =
2906                self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
2907
2908            let mut neon_temps = vec![];
2909            let neon_temp = self.acquire_temp_simd().ok_or_else(|| {
2910                CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
2911            })?;
2912            neon_temps.push(neon_temp);
2913
2914            self.assembler
2915                .emit_fmov(Size::S32, src_gpr, Size::S32, Location::SIMD(neon_temp))?;
2916            self.assembler.emit_cnt(neon_temp, neon_temp)?;
2917            self.assembler.emit_addv(neon_temp, neon_temp)?;
2918            self.assembler
2919                .emit_fmov(Size::S32, Location::SIMD(neon_temp), Size::S32, dst_gpr)?;
2920
2921            if ret != dst_gpr {
2922                self.move_location(Size::S32, dst_gpr, ret)?;
2923            }
2924
2925            for r in temps {
2926                self.release_gpr(r);
2927            }
2928
2929            for r in neon_temps {
2930                self.release_simd(r);
2931            }
2932        } else {
2933            let mut temps = vec![];
2934            let src =
2935                self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, loc, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
2936            let dest =
2937                self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
2938            let src = if src == loc {
2939                let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
2940                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
2941                })?;
2942                temps.push(tmp);
2943                self.assembler
2944                    .emit_mov(Size::S32, src, Location::GPR(tmp))?;
2945                Location::GPR(tmp)
2946            } else {
2947                src
2948            };
2949            let tmp = {
2950                let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
2951                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
2952                })?;
2953                temps.push(tmp);
2954                Location::GPR(tmp)
2955            };
2956            let label_loop = self.assembler.get_label();
2957            let label_exit = self.assembler.get_label();
2958            self.assembler
2959                .emit_mov(Size::S32, Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp), dest)?; // 0 => dest
2960            self.assembler.emit_cbz_label(Size::S32, src, label_exit)?; // src==0, exit
2961            self.assembler.emit_label(label_loop)?; // loop:
2962            self.assembler
2963                .emit_add(Size::S32, dest, Location::Imm8(1), dest)?; // dest += 1
2964            self.assembler.emit_clz(Size::S32, src, tmp)?; // clz src => tmp
2965            self.assembler.emit_lsl(Size::S32, src, tmp, src)?; // src << tmp => src
2966            self.assembler
2967                .emit_lsl(Size::S32, src, Location::Imm8(1), src)?; // src << 1 => src
2968            self.assembler.emit_cbnz_label(Size::S32, src, label_loop)?; // if src!=0 goto loop
2969            self.assembler.emit_label(label_exit)?;
2970            if ret != dest {
2971                self.move_location(Size::S32, dest, ret)?;
2972            }
2973            for r in temps {
2974                self.release_gpr(r);
2975            }
2976        }
2977        Ok(())
2978    }
2979    fn i32_shl(
2980        &mut self,
2981        loc_a: Location,
2982        loc_b: Location,
2983        ret: Location,
2984    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
2985        self.emit_relaxed_binop3(
2986            Assembler::emit_lsl,
2987            Size::S32,
2988            loc_a,
2989            loc_b,
2990            ret,
2991            ImmType::Shift32No0,
2992        )
2993    }
2994    fn i32_shr(
2995        &mut self,
2996        loc_a: Location,
2997        loc_b: Location,
2998        ret: Location,
2999    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
3000        self.emit_relaxed_binop3(
3001            Assembler::emit_lsr,
3002            Size::S32,
3003            loc_a,
3004            loc_b,
3005            ret,
3006            ImmType::Shift32No0,
3007        )

3009    fn i32_sar(
3010        &mut self,
3011        loc_a: Location,
3012        loc_b: Location,
3013        ret: Location,
3014    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
3015        self.emit_relaxed_binop3(
3016            Assembler::emit_asr,
3017            Size::S32,
3018            loc_a,
3019            loc_b,
3020            ret,
3021            ImmType::Shift32No0,
3022        )
3023    }
3024    fn i32_rol(
3025        &mut self,
3026        loc_a: Location,
3027        loc_b: Location,
3028        ret: Location,
3029    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
3030        let mut temps = vec![];
3031        let src2 = match loc_b {
3032            Location::Imm8(imm) => Location::Imm8(32 - (imm & 31)),
3033            Location::Imm32(imm) => Location::Imm8(32 - (imm & 31) as u8),
3034            Location::Imm64(imm) => Location::Imm8(32 - (imm & 31) as u8),
3035            _ => {
3036                let tmp1 = self.location_to_reg(
3037                    Size::S32,
3038                    Location::Imm32(32),
3039                    &mut temps,
3040                    ImmType::None,
3041                    true,
3042                    None,
3043                )?;
3044                let tmp2 =
3045                    self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, loc_b, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
3046                self.assembler.emit_sub(Size::S32, tmp1, tmp2, tmp1)?;
3047                tmp1
3048            }
3049        };
3050        self.emit_relaxed_binop3(
3051            Assembler::emit_ror,
3052            Size::S32,
3053            loc_a,
3054            src2,
3055            ret,
3056            ImmType::Shift32No0,
3057        )?;
3058        for r in temps {
3059            self.release_gpr(r);
3060        }
3061        Ok(())
3062    }

3064        &mut self,
3065        loc_a: Location,
3066        loc_b: Location,
3067        ret: Location,
3068    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
3069        self.emit_relaxed_binop3(
3070            Assembler::emit_ror,
3071            Size::S32,
3072            loc_a,
3073            loc_b,
3074            ret,
3075            ImmType::Shift32No0,
3076        )
3077    }

3417    // i32 atomic Add with i32
3418    fn i32_atomic_add(
3419        &mut self,
3420        loc: Location,
3421        target: Location,
3422        memarg: &MemArg,
3423        ret: Location,
3424        need_check: bool,
3425        imported_memories: bool,
3426        offset: i32,
3427        heap_access_oob: Label,
3428        unaligned_atomic: Label,
3429    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
3430        self.memory_op(
3431            target,
3432            memarg,
3433            true,
3434            4,
3435            need_check,
3436            imported_memories,
3437            offset,
3438            heap_access_oob,
3439            unaligned_atomic,
3440            |this, addr| {
3441                let mut temps = vec![];
3442                let tmp1 = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
3443                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
3444                })?;
3445                let tmp2 = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
3446                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
3447                })?;
3448                let dst =
3449                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S32, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
3450                let reread = this.get_label();
3451
3452                this.emit_label(reread)?;
3453                this.assembler
3454                    .emit_ldaxr(Size::S32, dst, Location::GPR(addr))?;
3455                this.emit_binop_add32(dst, loc, Location::GPR(tmp1))?;
3456                this.assembler.emit_stlxr(
3457                    Size::S32,
3458                    Location::GPR(tmp2),
3459                    Location::GPR(tmp1),
3460                    Location::GPR(addr),
3461                )?;
3462                this.assembler
3463                    .emit_cbnz_label(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp2), reread)?;
3464                this.assembler.emit_dmb()?;
3465
3466                if dst != ret {
3467                    this.move_location(Size::S32, ret, dst)?;
3468                }
3469                for r in temps {
3470                    this.release_gpr(r);
3471                }
3472                this.release_gpr(tmp1);
3473                this.release_gpr(tmp2);
3474                Ok(())
3475            },
3476        )
3477    }

3600    // i32 atomic Sub with i32
3601    fn i32_atomic_sub(
3602        &mut self,
3603        loc: Location,
3604        target: Location,
3605        memarg: &MemArg,
3606        ret: Location,
3607        need_check: bool,
3608        imported_memories: bool,
3609        offset: i32,
3610        heap_access_oob: Label,
3611        unaligned_atomic: Label,
3612    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
3613        self.memory_op(
3614            target,
3615            memarg,
3616            true,
3617            4,
3618            need_check,
3619            imported_memories,
3620            offset,
3621            heap_access_oob,
3622            unaligned_atomic,
3623            |this, addr| {
3624                let mut temps = vec![];
3625                let tmp1 = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
3626                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
3627                })?;
3628                let tmp2 = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
3629                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
3630                })?;
3631                let dst =
3632                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S32, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
3633                let reread = this.get_label();
3634
3635                this.emit_label(reread)?;
3636                this.assembler
3637                    .emit_ldaxr(Size::S32, dst, Location::GPR(addr))?;
3638                this.emit_binop_sub32(dst, loc, Location::GPR(tmp1))?;
3639                this.assembler.emit_stlxr(
3640                    Size::S32,
3641                    Location::GPR(tmp2),
3642                    Location::GPR(tmp1),
3643                    Location::GPR(addr),
3644                )?;
3645                this.assembler
3646                    .emit_cbnz_label(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp2), reread)?;
3647                this.assembler.emit_dmb()?;
3648
3649                if dst != ret {
3650                    this.move_location(Size::S32, ret, dst)?;
3651                }
3652                for r in temps {
3653                    this.release_gpr(r);
3654                }
3655                this.release_gpr(tmp1);
3656                this.release_gpr(tmp2);
3657                Ok(())
3658            },
3659        )
3660    }

4276        memarg: &MemArg,
4277        ret: Location,
4278        need_check: bool,
4279        imported_memories: bool,
4280        offset: i32,
4281        heap_access_oob: Label,
4282        unaligned_atomic: Label,
4283    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
4284        self.memory_op(
4285            target,
4286            memarg,
4287            true,
4288            2,
4289            need_check,
4290            imported_memories,
4291            offset,
4292            heap_access_oob,
4293            unaligned_atomic,
4294            |this, addr| {
4295                let mut temps = vec![];
4296                let tmp1 = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
4297                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
4298                })?;
4299                let tmp2 = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
4300                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
4301                })?;
4302                let dst =
4303                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S32, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
4304                let reread = this.get_label();
4305
4306                this.emit_label(reread)?;
4307                this.assembler
4308                    .emit_ldaxrh(Size::S32, dst, Location::GPR(addr))?;
4309                this.emit_binop_xor32(dst, loc, Location::GPR(tmp1))?;
4310                this.assembler.emit_stlxrh(
4311                    Size::S32,
4312                    Location::GPR(tmp2),
4313                    Location::GPR(tmp1),
4314                    Location::GPR(addr),
4315                )?;
4316                this.assembler
4317                    .emit_cbnz_label(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp2), reread)?;
4318                this.assembler.emit_dmb()?;
4319
4320                if dst != ret {
4321                    this.move_location(Size::S32, ret, dst)?;
4322                }
4323                for r in temps {
4324                    this.release_gpr(r);
4325                }
4326                this.release_gpr(tmp1);
4327                this.release_gpr(tmp2);
4328                Ok(())
4329            },
4330        )
4331    }

4506    // i32 atomic Exchange with i32
4507    fn i32_atomic_cmpxchg(
4508        &mut self,
4509        new: Location,
4510        cmp: Location,
4511        target: Location,
4512        memarg: &MemArg,
4513        ret: Location,
4514        need_check: bool,
4515        imported_memories: bool,
4516        offset: i32,
4517        heap_access_oob: Label,
4518        unaligned_atomic: Label,
4519    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
4520        self.memory_op(
4521            target,
4522            memarg,
4523            true,
4524            4,
4525            need_check,
4526            imported_memories,
4527            offset,
4528            heap_access_oob,
4529            unaligned_atomic,
4530            |this, addr| {
4531                let mut temps = vec![];
4532                let tmp = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
4533                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
4534                })?;
4535                let dst =
4536                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S32, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
4537                let org =
4538                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S32, new, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
4539                let reread = this.get_label();
4540                let nosame = this.get_label();
4541
4542                this.emit_label(reread)?;
4543                this.assembler
4544                    .emit_ldaxr(Size::S32, dst, Location::GPR(addr))?;
4545                this.emit_relaxed_cmp(Size::S32, dst, cmp)?;
4546                this.assembler.emit_bcond_label(Condition::Ne, nosame)?;
4547                this.assembler.emit_stlxr(
4548                    Size::S32,
4549                    Location::GPR(tmp),
4550                    org,
4551                    Location::GPR(addr),
4552                )?;
4553                this.assembler
4554                    .emit_cbnz_label(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp), reread)?;
4555                this.assembler.emit_dmb()?;
4556
4557                this.emit_label(nosame)?;
4558                if dst != ret {
4559                    this.move_location(Size::S32, ret, dst)?;
4560                }
4561                for r in temps {
4562                    this.release_gpr(r);
4563                }
4564                this.release_gpr(tmp);
4565                Ok(())
4566            },
4567        )
4568    }

4695
4696    fn emit_call_with_reloc(
4697        &mut self,
4698        _calling_convention: CallingConvention,
4699        reloc_target: RelocationTarget,
4700    ) -> Result<Vec<Relocation>, CompileError> {
4701        let mut relocations = vec![];
4702        let next = self.get_label();
4703        let reloc_at = self.assembler.get_offset().0;
4704        self.emit_label(next)?; // this is to be sure the current imm26 value is 0
4705        self.assembler.emit_call_label(next)?;
4706        relocations.push(Relocation {
4707            kind: RelocationKind::Arm64Call,
4708            reloc_target,
4709            offset: reloc_at as u32,
4710            addend: 0,
4711        });
4712        Ok(relocations)
4713    }

4715    fn emit_binop_add64(
4716        &mut self,
4717        loc_a: Location,
4718        loc_b: Location,
4719        ret: Location,
4720    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
4721        self.emit_relaxed_binop3(
4722            Assembler::emit_add,
4723            Size::S64,
4724            loc_a,
4725            loc_b,
4726            ret,
4727            ImmType::Bits12,
4728        )
4729    }

4745    fn emit_binop_mul64(
4746        &mut self,
4747        loc_a: Location,
4748        loc_b: Location,
4749        ret: Location,
4750    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
4751        self.emit_relaxed_binop3(
4752            Assembler::emit_mul,

4754            loc_a,
4755            loc_b,
4756            ret,
4757            ImmType::None,

4760    fn emit_binop_udiv64(
4761        &mut self,
4762        loc_a: Location,
4763        loc_b: Location,
4764        ret: Location,
4765        integer_division_by_zero: Label,
4766    ) -> Result<usize, CompileError> {
4767        let mut temps = vec![];
4768        let src1 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc_a, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
4769        let src2 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc_b, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
4770        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
4771
4772        self.assembler
4773            .emit_cbz_label(Size::S64, src2, integer_division_by_zero)?;
4774        let offset = self.mark_instruction_with_trap_code(TrapCode::IntegerOverflow);
4775        self.assembler.emit_udiv(Size::S64, src1, src2, dest)?;
4776        if ret != dest {
4777            self.move_location(Size::S64, dest, ret)?;
4778        }
4779        for r in temps {
4780            self.release_gpr(r);
4781        }
4782        Ok(offset)
4783    }
4784    fn emit_binop_sdiv64(
4785        &mut self,
4786        loc_a: Location,
4787        loc_b: Location,
4788        ret: Location,
4789        integer_division_by_zero: Label,
4790        integer_overflow: Label,
4791    ) -> Result<usize, CompileError> {
4792        let mut temps = vec![];
4793        let src1 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc_a, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
4794        let src2 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc_b, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
4795        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
4796
4797        self.assembler
4798            .emit_cbz_label_far(Size::S64, src2, integer_division_by_zero)?;
4799        let label_nooverflow = self.assembler.get_label();
4800        let tmp = self.location_to_reg(
4801            Size::S64,
4802            Location::Imm64(0x8000000000000000),
4803            &mut temps,
4804            ImmType::None,
4805            true,
4806            None,
4807        )?;
4808        self.assembler.emit_cmp(Size::S64, tmp, src1)?;
4809        self.assembler
4810            .emit_bcond_label(Condition::Ne, label_nooverflow)?;
4811        self.assembler.emit_movn(Size::S64, tmp, 0)?;
4812        self.assembler.emit_cmp(Size::S64, tmp, src2)?;
4813        self.assembler
4814            .emit_bcond_label_far(Condition::Eq, integer_overflow)?;
4815        let offset = self.mark_instruction_with_trap_code(TrapCode::IntegerOverflow);
4816        self.assembler.emit_label(label_nooverflow)?;
4817        self.assembler.emit_sdiv(Size::S64, src1, src2, dest)?;
4818        if ret != dest {
4819            self.move_location(Size::S64, dest, ret)?;
4820        }
4821        for r in temps {
4822            self.release_gpr(r);
4823        }
4824        Ok(offset)
4825    }
4826    fn emit_binop_urem64(
4827        &mut self,
4828        loc_a: Location,
4829        loc_b: Location,
4830        ret: Location,
4831        integer_division_by_zero: Label,
4832    ) -> Result<usize, CompileError> {
4833        let mut temps = vec![];
4834        let src1 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc_a, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
4835        let src2 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc_b, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
4836        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
4837        let dest = if dest == src1 || dest == src2 {
4838            let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
4839                CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
4840            })?;
4841            temps.push(tmp);
4842            self.assembler
4843                .emit_mov(Size::S32, dest, Location::GPR(tmp))?;
4844            Location::GPR(tmp)
4845        } else {
4846            dest
4847        };
4848        self.assembler
4849            .emit_cbz_label_far(Size::S64, src2, integer_division_by_zero)?;
4850        let offset = self.mark_instruction_with_trap_code(TrapCode::IntegerOverflow);
4851        self.assembler.emit_udiv(Size::S64, src1, src2, dest)?;
4852        // unsigned remainder : src1 - (src1/src2)*src2
4853        self.assembler
4854            .emit_msub(Size::S64, dest, src2, src1, dest)?;
4855        if ret != dest {
4856            self.move_location(Size::S64, dest, ret)?;
4857        }
4858        for r in temps {
4859            self.release_gpr(r);
4860        }
4861        Ok(offset)
4862    }
4863    fn emit_binop_srem64(
4864        &mut self,
4865        loc_a: Location,
4866        loc_b: Location,
4867        ret: Location,
4868        integer_division_by_zero: Label,
4869    ) -> Result<usize, CompileError> {
4870        let mut temps = vec![];
4871        let src1 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc_a, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
4872        let src2 = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc_b, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
4873        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
4874        let dest = if dest == src1 || dest == src2 {
4875            let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
4876                CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
4877            })?;
4878            temps.push(tmp);
4879            self.assembler
4880                .emit_mov(Size::S64, dest, Location::GPR(tmp))?;
4881            Location::GPR(tmp)
4882        } else {
4883            dest
4884        };
4885        self.assembler
4886            .emit_cbz_label_far(Size::S64, src2, integer_division_by_zero)?;
4887        let offset = self.mark_instruction_with_trap_code(TrapCode::IntegerOverflow);
4888        self.assembler.emit_sdiv(Size::S64, src1, src2, dest)?;
4889        // unsigned remainder : src1 - (src1/src2)*src2
4890        self.assembler
4891            .emit_msub(Size::S64, dest, src2, src1, dest)?;
4892        if ret != dest {
4893            self.move_location(Size::S64, dest, ret)?;
4894        }
4895        for r in temps {
4896            self.release_gpr(r);
4897        }
4898        Ok(offset)
4899    }
4900    fn emit_binop_and64(
4901        &mut self,
4902        loc_a: Location,
4903        loc_b: Location,
4904        ret: Location,
4905    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {

4907            Assembler::emit_and,

5025    fn i64_clz(&mut self, src: Location, dst: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
5026        self.emit_relaxed_binop(Assembler::emit_clz, Size::S64, src, dst, true)
5027    }
5028    fn i64_ctz(&mut self, src: Location, dst: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
5029        let mut temps = vec![];
5030        let src = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, src, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
5031        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, dst, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
5032        self.assembler.emit_rbit(Size::S64, src, dest)?;
5033        self.assembler.emit_clz(Size::S64, dest, dest)?;
5034        if dst != dest {
5035            self.move_location(Size::S64, dest, dst)?;
5036        }
5037        for r in temps {
5038            self.release_gpr(r);
5039        }
5040        Ok(())
5041    }
5042    fn i64_popcnt(&mut self, loc: Location, ret: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
5043        if self.has_neon {
5044            let mut temps = vec![];
5045
5046            let src_gpr =
5047                self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
5048            let dst_gpr =
5049                self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
5050
5051            let mut neon_temps = vec![];
5052            let neon_temp = self.acquire_temp_simd().ok_or_else(|| {
5053                CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
5054            })?;
5055            neon_temps.push(neon_temp);
5056
5057            self.assembler
5058                .emit_fmov(Size::S64, src_gpr, Size::S64, Location::SIMD(neon_temp))?;
5059            self.assembler.emit_cnt(neon_temp, neon_temp)?;
5060            self.assembler.emit_addv(neon_temp, neon_temp)?;
5061            self.assembler
5062                .emit_fmov(Size::S64, Location::SIMD(neon_temp), Size::S64, dst_gpr)?;
5063
5064            if ret != dst_gpr {
5065                self.move_location(Size::S64, dst_gpr, ret)?;
5066            }
5067
5068            for r in temps {
5069                self.release_gpr(r);
5070            }
5071
5072            for r in neon_temps {
5073                self.release_simd(r);
5074            }
5075        } else {
5076            let mut temps = vec![];
5077            let src =
5078                self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
5079            let dest =
5080                self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
5081            let src = if src == loc {
5082                let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
5083                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
5084                })?;
5085                temps.push(tmp);
5086                self.assembler
5087                    .emit_mov(Size::S64, src, Location::GPR(tmp))?;
5088                Location::GPR(tmp)
5089            } else {
5090                src
5091            };
5092            let tmp = {
5093                let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
5094                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
5095                })?;
5096                temps.push(tmp);
5097                Location::GPR(tmp)
5098            };
5099            let label_loop = self.assembler.get_label();
5100            let label_exit = self.assembler.get_label();
5101            self.assembler
5102                .emit_mov(Size::S32, Location::GPR(GPR::XzrSp), dest)?; // dest <= 0
5103            self.assembler.emit_cbz_label(Size::S64, src, label_exit)?; // src == 0, then goto label_exit
5104            self.assembler.emit_label(label_loop)?;
5105            self.assembler
5106                .emit_add(Size::S32, dest, Location::Imm8(1), dest)?; // dest += 1
5107            self.assembler.emit_clz(Size::S64, src, tmp)?; // clz src => tmp
5108            self.assembler.emit_lsl(Size::S64, src, tmp, src)?; // src << tmp => src
5109            self.assembler
5110                .emit_lsl(Size::S64, src, Location::Imm8(1), src)?; // src << 1 => src
5111            self.assembler.emit_cbnz_label(Size::S64, src, label_loop)?; // src != 0, then goto label_loop
5112            self.assembler.emit_label(label_exit)?;
5113            if ret != dest {
5114                self.move_location(Size::S64, dest, ret)?;
5115            }
5116            for r in temps {
5117                self.release_gpr(r);
5118            }
5119        }
5120
5121        Ok(())
5122    }

5168    fn i64_rol(
5169        &mut self,
5170        loc_a: Location,
5171        loc_b: Location,
5172        ret: Location,
5173    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
5174        // there is no ROL on ARM64. We use ROR with 64-value instead
5175        let mut temps = vec![];
5176        let src2 = match loc_b {
5177            Location::Imm8(imm) => Location::Imm8(64 - (imm & 63)),
5178            Location::Imm32(imm) => Location::Imm8(64 - (imm & 63) as u8),
5179            Location::Imm64(imm) => Location::Imm8(64 - (imm & 63) as u8),
5180            _ => {
5181                let tmp1 = self.location_to_reg(
5182                    Size::S64,
5183                    Location::Imm32(64),
5184                    &mut temps,
5185                    ImmType::None,
5186                    true,
5187                    None,
5188                )?;
5189                let tmp2 =
5190                    self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc_b, &mut temps, ImmType::None, true, None)?;
5191                self.assembler.emit_sub(Size::S64, tmp1, tmp2, tmp1)?;
5192                tmp1
5193            }
5194        };
5195        self.emit_relaxed_binop3(
5196            Assembler::emit_ror,
5197            Size::S64,
5198            loc_a,
5199            src2,
5200            ret,
5201            ImmType::Shift64No0,
5202        )?;
5203        for r in temps {
5204            self.release_gpr(r);
5205        }
5206        Ok(())
5207    }
5208    fn i64_ror(
5209        &mut self,
5210        loc_a: Location,
5211        loc_b: Location,
5212        ret: Location,
5213    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
5214        self.emit_relaxed_binop3(

5245        )
5246    }

5683    // i64 atomic Add with i64
5684    fn i64_atomic_add(
5685        &mut self,
5686        loc: Location,
5687        target: Location,
5688        memarg: &MemArg,
5689        ret: Location,
5690        need_check: bool,
5691        imported_memories: bool,
5692        offset: i32,
5693        heap_access_oob: Label,
5694        unaligned_atomic: Label,
5695    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
5696        self.memory_op(
5697            target,
5698            memarg,
5699            true,
5700            8,
5701            need_check,
5702            imported_memories,
5703            offset,
5704            heap_access_oob,
5705            unaligned_atomic,
5706            |this, addr| {
5707                let mut temps = vec![];
5708                let tmp1 = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
5709                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
5710                })?;
5711                let tmp2 = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
5712                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
5713                })?;
5714                let dst =
5715                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
5716                let reread = this.get_label();
5717
5718                this.emit_label(reread)?;
5719                this.assembler
5720                    .emit_ldaxr(Size::S64, dst, Location::GPR(addr))?;
5721                this.emit_binop_add64(dst, loc, Location::GPR(tmp1))?;
5722                this.assembler.emit_stlxr(
5723                    Size::S64,
5724                    Location::GPR(tmp2),
5725                    Location::GPR(tmp1),
5726                    Location::GPR(addr),
5727                )?;
5728                this.assembler
5729                    .emit_cbnz_label(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp2), reread)?;
5730                this.assembler.emit_dmb()?;
5731
5732                if dst != ret {
5733                    this.move_location(Size::S64, ret, dst)?;
5734                }
5735                for r in temps {
5736                    this.release_gpr(r);
5737                }
5738                this.release_gpr(tmp1);
5739                this.release_gpr(tmp2);
5740                Ok(())
5741            },
5742        )
5743    }

6207                this.assembler
6208                    .emit_ldaxr(Size::S64, dst, Location::GPR(addr))?;
6209                this.emit_binop_and64(dst, loc, Location::GPR(tmp1))?;
6210                this.assembler.emit_stlxr(
6211                    Size::S64,
6212                    Location::GPR(tmp2),
6213                    Location::GPR(tmp1),
6214                    Location::GPR(addr),
6215                )?;
6216                this.assembler
6217                    .emit_cbnz_label(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp2), reread)?;
6218                this.assembler.emit_dmb()?;
6219
6220                if dst != ret {
6221                    this.move_location(Size::S64, ret, dst)?;
6222                }
6223                for r in temps {
6224                    this.release_gpr(r);
6225                }
6226                this.release_gpr(tmp1);
6227                this.release_gpr(tmp2);
6228                Ok(())
6229            },
6230        )
6231    }
6232    // i64 atomic And with u8

6848        ret: Location,
6849        need_check: bool,
6850        imported_memories: bool,
6851        offset: i32,
6852        heap_access_oob: Label,
6853        unaligned_atomic: Label,
6854    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
6855        self.memory_op(
6856            target,
6857            memarg,
6858            true,
6859            4,
6860            need_check,
6861            imported_memories,
6862            offset,
6863            heap_access_oob,
6864            unaligned_atomic,
6865            |this, addr| {
6866                let mut temps = vec![];
6867                let tmp1 = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
6868                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
6869                })?;
6870                let tmp2 = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
6871                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
6872                })?;
6873                let dst =
6874                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
6875                let reread = this.get_label();
6876
6877                this.emit_label(reread)?;
6878                this.assembler
6879                    .emit_ldaxr(Size::S32, dst, Location::GPR(addr))?;
6880                this.emit_binop_xor64(dst, loc, Location::GPR(tmp1))?;
6881                this.assembler.emit_stlxr(
6882                    Size::S32,
6883                    Location::GPR(tmp2),
6884                    Location::GPR(tmp1),
6885                    Location::GPR(addr),
6886                )?;
6887                this.assembler
6888                    .emit_cbnz_label(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp2), reread)?;
6889                this.assembler.emit_dmb()?;
6890
6891                if dst != ret {
6892                    this.move_location(Size::S64, ret, dst)?;
6893                }
6894                for r in temps {
6895                    this.release_gpr(r);
6896                }
6897                this.release_gpr(tmp1);
6898                this.release_gpr(tmp2);
6899                Ok(())
6900            },
6901        )
6902    }

7135    // i64 atomic Exchange with i64
7136    fn i64_atomic_cmpxchg(
7137        &mut self,
7138        new: Location,
7139        cmp: Location,
7140        target: Location,
7141        memarg: &MemArg,
7142        ret: Location,
7143        need_check: bool,
7144        imported_memories: bool,
7145        offset: i32,
7146        heap_access_oob: Label,
7147        unaligned_atomic: Label,
7148    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7149        self.memory_op(
7150            target,
7151            memarg,
7152            true,
7153            8,
7154            need_check,
7155            imported_memories,
7156            offset,
7157            heap_access_oob,
7158            unaligned_atomic,
7159            |this, addr| {
7160                let mut temps = vec![];
7161                let tmp = this.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
7162                    CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
7163                })?;
7164                let dst =
7165                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
7166                let org =
7167                    this.location_to_reg(Size::S64, new, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
7168                let reread = this.get_label();
7169                let nosame = this.get_label();
7170
7171                this.emit_label(reread)?;
7172                this.assembler
7173                    .emit_ldaxr(Size::S64, dst, Location::GPR(addr))?;
7174                this.emit_relaxed_cmp(Size::S64, dst, cmp)?;
7175                this.assembler.emit_bcond_label(Condition::Ne, nosame)?;
7176                this.assembler.emit_stlxr(
7177                    Size::S64,
7178                    Location::GPR(tmp),
7179                    org,
7180                    Location::GPR(addr),
7181                )?;
7182                this.assembler
7183                    .emit_cbnz_label(Size::S32, Location::GPR(tmp), reread)?;
7184                this.assembler.emit_dmb()?;
7185
7186                this.emit_label(nosame)?;
7187                if dst != ret {
7188                    this.move_location(Size::S64, ret, dst)?;
7189                }
7190                for r in temps {
7191                    this.release_gpr(r);
7192                }
7193                this.release_gpr(tmp);
7194                Ok(())
7195            },
7196        )
7197    }

7388    fn f32_load(
7389        &mut self,
7390        addr: Location,
7391        memarg: &MemArg,
7392        ret: Location,
7393        need_check: bool,
7394        imported_memories: bool,
7395        offset: i32,
7396        heap_access_oob: Label,
7397        unaligned_atomic: Label,
7398    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7399        self.memory_op(
7400            addr,
7401            memarg,
7402            false,
7403            4,
7404            need_check,
7405            imported_memories,
7406            offset,
7407            heap_access_oob,
7408            unaligned_atomic,
7409            |this, addr| this.emit_relaxed_ldr32(Size::S32, ret, Location::Memory(addr, 0)),
7410        )
7411    }
7412    fn f32_save(
7413        &mut self,
7414        target_value: Location,
7415        memarg: &MemArg,
7416        target_addr: Location,
7417        canonicalize: bool,
7418        need_check: bool,
7419        imported_memories: bool,
7420        offset: i32,
7421        heap_access_oob: Label,
7422        unaligned_atomic: Label,
7423    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7424        let canonicalize = canonicalize && self.arch_supports_canonicalize_nan();
7425        self.memory_op(
7426            target_addr,
7427            memarg,
7428            false,
7429            4,
7430            need_check,
7431            imported_memories,
7432            offset,
7433            heap_access_oob,
7434            unaligned_atomic,
7435            |this, addr| {
7436                if !canonicalize {
7437                    this.emit_relaxed_str32(target_value, Location::Memory(addr, 0))
7438                } else {
7439                    this.canonicalize_nan(Size::S32, target_value, Location::Memory(addr, 0))
7440                }
7441            },
7442        )
7443    }

7500
7501    fn convert_f64_i64(
7502        &mut self,
7503        loc: Location,
7504        signed: bool,
7505        ret: Location,
7506    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7507        let mut gprs = vec![];
7508        let mut neons = vec![];
7509        let src = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, loc, &mut gprs, ImmType::NoneXzr, true, None)?;
7510        let dest = self.location_to_neon(Size::S64, ret, &mut neons, ImmType::None, false)?;
7511        if signed {
7512            self.assembler.emit_scvtf(Size::S64, src, Size::S64, dest)?;
7513        } else {
7514            self.assembler.emit_ucvtf(Size::S64, src, Size::S64, dest)?;
7515        }
7516        if ret != dest {
7517            self.move_location(Size::S64, dest, ret)?;
7518        }
7519        for r in gprs {
7520            self.release_gpr(r);
7521        }
7522        for r in neons {
7523            self.release_simd(r);
7524        }
7525        Ok(())
7526    }
7527    fn convert_f64_i32(
7528        &mut self,

7605    fn convert_i64_f64(
7606        &mut self,
7607        loc: Location,
7608        ret: Location,
7609        signed: bool,
7610        sat: bool,
7611    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7612        let mut gprs = vec![];
7613        let mut neons = vec![];
7614        let src = self.location_to_neon(Size::S64, loc, &mut neons, ImmType::None, true)?;
7615        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut gprs, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
7616        let old_fpcr = if !sat {
7617            self.reset_exception_fpsr()?;
7618            self.set_trap_enabled(&mut gprs)?
7619        } else {
7620            GPR::XzrSp
7621        };
7622        if signed {
7623            self.assembler
7624                .emit_fcvtzs(Size::S64, src, Size::S64, dest)?;
7625        } else {
7626            self.assembler
7627                .emit_fcvtzu(Size::S64, src, Size::S64, dest)?;
7628        }
7629        if !sat {
7630            self.trap_float_convertion_errors(old_fpcr, Size::S64, src, &mut gprs)?;
7631        }
7632        if ret != dest {
7633            self.move_location(Size::S64, dest, ret)?;
7634        }
7635        for r in gprs {
7636            self.release_gpr(r);
7637        }
7638        for r in neons {
7639            self.release_simd(r);
7640        }
7641        Ok(())
7642    }
7643    fn convert_i32_f64(
7644        &mut self,

7646        ret: Location,

7658            GPR::XzrSp
7659        };

7661            self.assembler
7662                .emit_fcvtzs(Size::S64, src, Size::S32, dest)?;
7663        } else {
7664            self.assembler
7665                .emit_fcvtzu(Size::S64, src, Size::S32, dest)?;
7666        }

7671            self.move_location(Size::S32, dest, ret)?;

7757    fn convert_f64_f32(&mut self, loc: Location, ret: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7758        self.emit_relaxed_binop_neon(Assembler::emit_fcvt, Size::S32, loc, ret, true)
7759    }
7760    fn convert_f32_f64(&mut self, loc: Location, ret: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7761        self.emit_relaxed_binop_neon(Assembler::emit_fcvt, Size::S64, loc, ret, true)
7762    }
7763    fn f64_neg(&mut self, loc: Location, ret: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7764        self.emit_relaxed_binop_neon(Assembler::emit_fneg, Size::S64, loc, ret, true)
7765    }
7766    fn f64_abs(&mut self, loc: Location, ret: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7767        let tmp = self.acquire_temp_gpr().ok_or_else(|| {
7768            CompileError::Codegen("singlepass cannot acquire temp gpr".to_owned())
7769        })?;
7770
7771        self.move_location(Size::S64, loc, Location::GPR(tmp))?;
7772        self.assembler.emit_and(
7773            Size::S64,
7774            Location::GPR(tmp),
7775            Location::Imm64(0x7fffffffffffffffu64),
7776            Location::GPR(tmp),
7777        )?;
7778        self.move_location(Size::S64, Location::GPR(tmp), ret)?;
7779
7780        self.release_gpr(tmp);
7781        Ok(())
7782    }
7783    fn emit_i64_copysign(&mut self, tmp1: GPR, tmp2: GPR) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7784        self.assembler.emit_and(
7785            Size::S64,
7786            Location::GPR(tmp1),
7787            Location::Imm64(0x7fffffffffffffffu64),
7788            Location::GPR(tmp1),
7789        )?;
7790
7791        self.assembler.emit_and(
7792            Size::S64,
7793            Location::GPR(tmp2),
7794            Location::Imm64(0x8000000000000000u64),
7795            Location::GPR(tmp2),
7796        )?;
7797
7798        self.assembler.emit_or(
7799            Size::S64,
7800            Location::GPR(tmp1),
7801            Location::GPR(tmp2),
7802            Location::GPR(tmp1),
7803        )
7804    }

7806        self.emit_relaxed_binop_neon(Assembler::emit_fsqrt, Size::S64, loc, ret, true)
7807    }

7820    fn f64_cmp_ge(
7821        &mut self,
7822        loc_a: Location,
7823        loc_b: Location,
7824        ret: Location,
7825    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7826        let mut temps = vec![];
7827        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S64, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
7828        self.emit_relaxed_binop_neon(Assembler::emit_fcmp, Size::S64, loc_b, loc_a, false)?;
7829        self.assembler.emit_cset(Size::S32, dest, Condition::Ls)?;
7830        if ret != dest {
7831            self.move_location(Size::S32, dest, ret)?;
7832        }
7833        for r in temps {
7834            self.release_gpr(r);
7835        }
7836        Ok(())
7837    }

7847        self.assembler.emit_cset(Size::S32, dest, Condition::Cc)?;

7849            self.move_location(Size::S32, dest, ret)?;

7855    }

7928    fn f64_min(
7929        &mut self,
7930        loc_a: Location,
7931        loc_b: Location,
7932        ret: Location,
7933    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
7934        let mut temps = vec![];
7935        let old_fpcr = self.set_default_nan(&mut temps)?;
7936        self.emit_relaxed_binop3_neon(
7937            Assembler::emit_fmin,
7938            Size::S64,
7939            loc_a,
7940            loc_b,
7941            ret,
7942            ImmType::None,
7943        )?;
7944        self.restore_fpcr(old_fpcr)?;
7945        for r in temps {
7946            self.release_gpr(r);
7947        }
7948        Ok(())
7949    }

8078    }
8079    fn f32_floor(&mut self, loc: Location, ret: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
8080        self.emit_relaxed_binop_neon(Assembler::emit_frintm, Size::S32, loc, ret, true)
8081    }
8082    fn f32_nearest(&mut self, loc: Location, ret: Location) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
8083        self.emit_relaxed_binop_neon(Assembler::emit_frintn, Size::S32, loc, ret, true)
8084    }
8085    fn f32_cmp_ge(
8086        &mut self,
8087        loc_a: Location,
8088        loc_b: Location,
8089        ret: Location,
8090    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
8091        let mut temps = vec![];
8092        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
8093        self.emit_relaxed_binop_neon(Assembler::emit_fcmp, Size::S32, loc_b, loc_a, false)?;
8094        self.assembler.emit_cset(Size::S32, dest, Condition::Ls)?;
8095        if ret != dest {
8096            self.move_location(Size::S32, dest, ret)?;
8097        }
8098        for r in temps {
8099            self.release_gpr(r);
8100        }
8101        Ok(())
8102    }
8103    fn f32_cmp_gt(
8104        &mut self,
8105        loc_a: Location,
8106        loc_b: Location,
8107        ret: Location,
8108    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
8109        let mut temps = vec![];
8110        let dest = self.location_to_reg(Size::S32, ret, &mut temps, ImmType::None, false, None)?;
8111        self.emit_relaxed_binop_neon(Assembler::emit_fcmp, Size::S32, loc_b, loc_a, false)?;
8112        self.assembler.emit_cset(Size::S32, dest, Condition::Cc)?;
8113        if ret != dest {
8114            self.move_location(Size::S32, dest, ret)?;
8115        }
8116        for r in temps {
8117            self.release_gpr(r);
8118        }
8119        Ok(())
8120    }

8193    fn f32_min(
8194        &mut self,
8195        loc_a: Location,
8196        loc_b: Location,
8197        ret: Location,
8198    ) -> Result<(), CompileError> {
8199        let mut temps = vec![];
8200        let old_fpcr = self.set_default_nan(&mut temps)?;
8201        self.emit_relaxed_binop3_neon(
8202            Assembler::emit_fmin,
8203            Size::S32,
8204            loc_a,
8205            loc_b,
8206            ret,
8207            ImmType::None,
8208        )?;
8209        self.restore_fpcr(old_fpcr)?;
8210        for r in temps {
8211            self.release_gpr(r);
8212        }
8213        Ok(())
8214    }
8215    fn f32_max(
8216        &mut self,

8230        )?;

8236    }

8324    #[cfg(feature = "unwind")]
8325    fn gen_dwarf_unwind_info(&mut self, code_len: usize) -> Option<UnwindInstructions> {
8326        let mut instructions = vec![];
8327        for &(instruction_offset, ref inst) in &self.unwind_ops {
8328            let instruction_offset = instruction_offset as u32;
8329            match *inst {
8330                UnwindOps::PushFP { up_to_sp } => {
8331                    instructions.push((
8332                        instruction_offset,
8333                        CallFrameInstruction::CfaOffset(up_to_sp as i32),
8334                    ));
8335                    instructions.push((
8336                        instruction_offset,
8337                        CallFrameInstruction::Offset(AArch64::X29, -(up_to_sp as i32)),
8338                    ));
8339                }
8340                UnwindOps::Push2Regs {
8341                    reg1,
8342                    reg2,
8343                    up_to_sp,
8344                } => {
8345                    instructions.push((
8346                        instruction_offset,
8347                        CallFrameInstruction::CfaOffset(up_to_sp as i32),
8348                    ));
8349                    instructions.push((
8350                        instruction_offset,
8351                        CallFrameInstruction::Offset(reg2.dwarf_index(), -(up_to_sp as i32) + 8),
8352                    ));
8353                    instructions.push((
8354                        instruction_offset,
8355                        CallFrameInstruction::Offset(reg1.dwarf_index(), -(up_to_sp as i32)),
8356                    ));
8357                }
8358                UnwindOps::DefineNewFrame => {
8359                    instructions.push((
8360                        instruction_offset,
8361                        CallFrameInstruction::CfaRegister(AArch64::X29),
8362                    ));
8363                }
8364                UnwindOps::SaveRegister { reg, bp_neg_offset } => instructions.push((
8365                    instruction_offset,
8366                    CallFrameInstruction::Offset(reg.dwarf_index(), -bp_neg_offset),
8367                )),
8368            }
8369        }
8370        Some(UnwindInstructions {
8371            instructions,
8372            len: code_len as u32,
8373        })
8374    }
8375    #[cfg(not(feature = "unwind"))]
8376    fn gen_dwarf_unwind_info(&mut self, _code_len: usize) -> Option<UnwindInstructions> {
8377        None
8378    }
8379
8380    fn gen_windows_unwind_info(&mut self, _code_len: usize) -> Option<Vec<u8>> {
8381        None
8382    }
8383}

8675    #[test]
8676    fn tests_arm64() -> Result<(), CompileError> {
8677        let mut machine = MachineARM64::new(None);
8678
8679        test_move_location(&mut machine, Size::S32)?;
8680        test_move_location(&mut machine, Size::S64)?;
8681        test_move_location_extended(&mut machine, false, Size::S8)?;
8682        test_move_location_extended(&mut machine, false, Size::S16)?;
8683        test_move_location_extended(&mut machine, false, Size::S32)?;
8684        test_move_location_extended(&mut machine, true, Size::S8)?;
8685        test_move_location_extended(&mut machine, true, Size::S16)?;
8686        test_move_location_extended(&mut machine, true, Size::S32)?;
8687        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_add32)?;
8688        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_add64)?;
8689        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_sub32)?;
8690        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_sub64)?;
8691        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_and32)?;
8692        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_and64)?;
8693        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_xor32)?;
8694        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_xor64)?;
8695        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_or32)?;
8696        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_or64)?;
8697        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_mul32)?;
8698        test_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::emit_binop_mul64)?;
8699        test_float_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::f32_add)?;
8700        test_float_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::f32_sub)?;
8701        test_float_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::f32_mul)?;
8702        test_float_binop_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::f32_div)?;
8703        test_float_cmp_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::f32_cmp_eq)?;
8704        test_float_cmp_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::f32_cmp_lt)?;
8705        test_float_cmp_op(&mut machine, MachineARM64::f32_cmp_le)?;
8706
8707        Ok(())
8708    }
8709}
